# CONCEPT 1 — GRWM

**Concept Line:** "Six months of silence ends tonight in the same room where it started."
**Format:** GRWM (Get Ready With Me)
**Stakes:** Getting ready for the dinner where I'll see him again after six months — and he doesn't know I'm coming
**Register:** KNOWING
**Duration:** 48 seconds total
**Frames:** 6 frames x 8 seconds each
**Wardrobe Pillar:** Pillar 5 (Evening Defined) — deep emerald silk slip dress, bias-cut, thin straps, floor-length with subtle side slit
**Hair:** HC-4 Soft Hollywood waves — deep side-parted, cascading over left shoulder, warm highlights catching light
**Makeup:** ML-17 Berry Sultry — berry-stained lip, smoked plum crease, luminous bronze skin, defined contour
**Setting:** GRWM Pillar 3 — Bedroom Golden Hour (full-length leaning mirror, golden shaft from west-facing window, bed with outfit laid, warm haze)
**Music:** Jazz-noir sultry electronic, 95 BPM, bass-forward, saxophone sample, muted snare
**Opener:** "Chh mahine... aur aaj, same room."
**Sign-off:** "Theek hai. His loss."
**Voice Mode:** SPOKEN
**Signature Flag:** FULL
**Energy Arc:** Vulnerable (Frame 1) > Processing (Frames 2-3) > Decision (Frame 4) > Ready (Frame 5) > Loose (Frame 6)

## IMAGE PROMPTS

### Frame 1 — Opening State (Bare Face, Stakes Declared)

ASPECT RATIO: 9:16 vertical. SUBJECT: AIRA — Adult woman late 20s-early 30s, South Asian (Indian), warm honey-to-caramel skin tone with golden undertone, 5'6"-5'8", soft-strong hourglass-athletic silhouette, fuller sculpted legs with toned thigh definition, fuller shapely thighs, fuller feminine arms with subtle muscle tone, fuller defined chest in proportion, flat toned midsection, defined waist clear waist-to-hip ratio, curvy hip line with natural feminine flare, heart-shaped to oval face, defined cheekbones, full defined lips with natural cupid's bow, almond-shaped expressive eyes dark brown iris with subtle amber flecks, strong but feminine groomed naturally arched brow, natural sun-kissed glow, long dark brown to near-black hair with subtle warm highlights naturally textured soft waves with body and movement, elegant well-groomed hands.

WARDROBE STATE (Frame 1): Cream silk robe loosely tied at waist, falling off left shoulder revealing bare collarbone and camisole strap beneath. Fabric catches golden light with visible weave texture. Robe hem at mid-thigh, legs bare, seated on bed edge.

HAIR STATE (Frame 1): Freshly washed, damp at ends, air-drying with natural wave forming, no product yet, no styling yet. Hair pushed behind right ear exposing full face, left side falling forward past shoulder. Slight frizz at crown from humidity.

MAKEUP STATE (Frame 1): Completely bare face. No foundation, no concealer, no color. Natural skin texture visible — slight under-eye softness, natural pore visibility on nose and cheeks, bare lips slightly dry with natural pink undertone, natural brow shape without product (slight asymmetry, left brow marginally higher), bare lashes with natural curl, no liner. Sun-kissed glow only from natural skin.

HAND POSITIONS: Right hand resting on right knee, fingers relaxed and slightly curled, elegant nails in bare natural finish. Left hand mid-motion tucking hair behind left ear, fingertips touching the strand at temple height, ring finger and pinky slightly extended.

FACIAL MICRO-DYNAMICS: Eyes — direct gaze to camera through full-length mirror reflection, slight squint from golden hour light streaming from camera-left window, right eye marginally more open than left (natural asymmetry), catchlight positioned at 10 o'clock in both irises from window key, inner-eye moisture catching warm amber light, lower lid micro-tension from soft knowing half-smile beginning. Brows — left brow lifted 2mm higher than right (knowing expression building), slight inner-brow draw suggesting thought-processing, brow hair direction natural and ungroomed. Lips — pre-smile tension at right corner lifting first (asymmetric Duchenne sequencing beginning in eyes before mouth), bottom lip slightly fuller from natural rest, lip-corner asymmetry with right side 1mm higher, slight lip-part on exhale revealing edge of upper teeth. Cheeks — apple-of-cheek beginning to lift with emerging smile, natural flush visible on bare skin at cheekbone, single subtle expression line forming at left nasolabial. Jaw — jaw softened and relaxed, throat-swallow visible as she gathers thought before speaking, neck tendon slight flex from head being tilted 5 degrees right. Breath — visible inhale lifting chest and left shoulder slightly, exhale about to begin as opener line forms.

BODY POSTURE: Seated on bed edge, weight distributed slightly left with left hip bearing more, right leg crossed over left at mid-calf, spine softly curved forward in intimate lean toward mirror, shoulders asymmetric (left dropped where robe slips, right slightly raised), hip angle creating natural feminine curve even seated. Left foot bare, toes curled slightly against hardwood floor. Right foot tucked behind left ankle.

KINETIC STILLNESS — Six Layers:
1. Subject micro-action: Mid-exhale, hair-tuck gesture caught at 70% completion, slight forward lean toward mirror as if about to speak
2. Fabric/hair state: Robe silk catching light with single fold mid-settle on left thigh, hair strand mid-swing from tuck gesture moving left-to-right, damp ends with one droplet at terminal point about to release
3. Particulate layer: Golden dust motes suspended in window light shaft crossing midground diagonally from upper-left to lower-right, 15-20 particles visible at various depths catching warm backlight
4. Contact-point activity: Fingertips pressing into hair strand creating slight indent, weight compression on mattress edge visible as fabric depression, bare foot creating micro-pressure on hardwood floor
5. Background motion: Sheer curtain mid-billow inward from cracked window, slight sway rightward at 3/4 extension, outfit on bed (emerald silk dress) catching breeze with hem lifting 2cm, tree shadow on wall shifting
6. Light in motion: Golden hour shaft with visible warmth gradient moving across floor as sun descends, rim light wrap on right shoulder edge fluctuating with curtain movement, single lens flare streak at 45 degrees from window frame catch

SPATIAL LOGIC:
- FOREGROUND: Out-of-focus bed edge with emerald dress draped, catching golden light, fabric texture soft-blurred, providing color story and narrative anticipation. Occupies bottom-left 20% of frame.
- MIDGROUND: Aira seated at bed edge reflected in full-length leaning mirror, sharp focus, primary action plane. Mirror frame (aged brass) creates frame-within-frame composition.
- BACKGROUND: Bedroom beyond — window with sheer ivory curtain billowing, warm haze, bedside table with half-drunk chai mug and small jewelry box open (gold earrings visible), closet door ajar showing garment edges. Soft focus, warm-shifted, atmospheric perspective applied.

LIGHTING:
- Key: Natural golden hour window light from camera-left, 4:30 PM warmth, hard-to-medium hardness creating defined shadows, color temp 3200K amber-gold
- Fill: Ambient bounce from cream walls at -2 stops from key, soft and warm, filling shadow side gently
- Rim: Golden wrap on right shoulder and right side of hair from window reflection off mirror frame, thin bright line defining separation from background
- Practical: None in frame (natural light only)
- Light separation from BG: Subject 1.5+ stops brighter than background wall

FRAMING: MCU / Bust crop — top of head with 8% headroom to mid-chest (cutting through chest, not at joint). Subject occupies 75% of frame height. Lookroom standard with breathing space camera-right (direction of gaze into mirror). Camera height at eye level. Body angle: 3/4 turn toward mirror, face reflected back toward camera. Shot composed through mirror reflection — we see Aira's reflection as primary subject with edge of her physical shoulder in far left of frame.

LENS: 50mm intimate portrait. APERTURE: f/2.0 creating shallow DOF — subject tack-sharp, foreground dress soft-blurred, background soft with bokeh circles from jewelry box and window light. Bokeh shape: round, warm-tinted.

COMPOSITION REFERENCE: Frame-within-frame (mirror as compositional device), Bradford Young skin-priority ambient soft approach, golden ratio placement with Aira's eyes at upper-right intersection.

ATMOSPHERE: Warm golden haze filling room, visible light shaft, intimate morning-after-shower humidity, dust motes as life-confirmation. Film grain: Kodak Portra 400 warmth.

COLOR GRADE: Warm amber midtones, honey-gold highlights, shadows lifted to warm chocolate-brown never true black, skin tones prioritized with golden undertone enhanced, slight desaturation on background elements to push subject forward. Overall Kodak Portra 400 warmth with Bradford Young skin-luminosity approach.

NEGATIVE: mirrored, flipped, inverted, extra limbs, fused fingers, melted features, asymmetric eyes (unintentional), garbled text, floating shadows, duplicated subjects, low-res patches, plastic skin, oversharpened, AI-generated artifacts, watermarks, signature, deformed hands, malformed teeth, joint cuts at ankle/knee/wrist/elbow/neck, amputated fingertips, cross-eyed, lazy eye, off-axis pupils, melted clothing, shoes-not-touching-ground, mismatched footwear pair, mannequin-stiff posture, dead eyes, statue-frozen energy.


### Frame 2 — First Application (Skincare + Foundation Base)

ASPECT RATIO: 9:16 vertical. SUBJECT: AIRA — Adult woman late 20s-early 30s, South Asian (Indian), warm honey-to-caramel skin tone with golden undertone, 5'6"-5'8", soft-strong hourglass-athletic silhouette, fuller sculpted legs with toned thigh definition, fuller shapely thighs, fuller feminine arms with subtle muscle tone, fuller defined chest in proportion, flat toned midsection, defined waist clear waist-to-hip ratio, curvy hip line with natural feminine flare, heart-shaped to oval face, defined cheekbones, full defined lips with natural cupid's bow, almond-shaped expressive eyes dark brown iris with subtle amber flecks, strong but feminine groomed naturally arched brow, natural sun-kissed glow, long dark brown to near-black hair with subtle warm highlights naturally textured soft waves with body and movement, elegant well-groomed hands.

WARDROBE STATE (Frame 2): Same cream silk robe, now both shoulders covered but loosely draped, sash slightly tighter from standing and resitting at vanity. Fabric pooling at lap.

HAIR STATE (Frame 2): Still damp-drying, now pushed fully behind both ears for application access. Natural wave pattern emerging more defined as hair dries. No styling product yet. One strand escaped at right temple.

MAKEUP STATE (Frame 2 — cumulative): Skincare applied (dewy sheen visible on skin surface from moisturizer), primer smoothed across T-zone giving slight blur effect to pore area. Foundation being actively applied — right cheek and forehead show smooth even coverage, left cheek still showing bare skin transition line where sponge hasn't reached yet. Brows still bare. Lips still bare with balm applied (slight sheen). No eye makeup.

HAND POSITIONS: Right hand holding damp beauty sponge mid-bounce against left cheekbone, fingers wrapped around sponge with thumb and index creating grip, wrist angled inward. Left hand holding glass bottle of liquid foundation (label reading "serum foundation" in elegant minimal typography), bottle resting in palm with fingers curled around base, held at mid-chest height with label facing camera.

FACIAL MICRO-DYNAMICS: Eyes — flicking upward to camera mid-application (intimacy lock moment), gaze caught between mirror-check and camera-address, right eye slightly narrowed from sponge pressure on left cheek pushing facial geometry, catchlight now at 11 o'clock from shifted head angle, amber flecks in iris catching golden side-light. Brows — both relaxed and natural during application focus, right brow micro-raised in conversational expression while speaking about stakes, left brow steady. Lips — soft smile forming while talking, bottom lip caught between words (phoneme shape of mid-sentence), lip-corner right side lifted in knowing half-smile, slight teeth visible at center where lips part for speech, lip balm sheen catching highlight. Cheeks — right cheek smooth with foundation, left cheek mid-transition showing bare-to-covered gradient, apple lift from speaking-smile. Jaw — slightly dropped for speech, relaxed, chin tilted 3 degrees down for application access. Breath — mid-exhale settling, chest still, shoulders relaxed and even.

BODY POSTURE: Seated at vanity surface (white marble top), weight centered, both feet flat on hardwood floor, torso upright with slight forward lean toward mirror, shoulders level and relaxed, spine straight with natural lumbar curve. Knees together, robe draped across lap.

KINETIC STILLNESS — Six Layers:
1. Subject micro-action: Sponge mid-bounce on cheekbone, caught at compression point, slight skin depression visible under sponge edge, head held steady for application
2. Fabric/hair state: Robe sleeve falling down right forearm as arm is raised for application, silk sliding with gravity direction downward, escaped hair strand at right temple mid-sway from head micro-adjustment
3. Particulate layer: Dust motes in golden shaft now shifted angle as time progresses, foundation micro-mist visible in air near sponge from bounce-release, 8-10 golden particles in light beam
4. Contact-point activity: Sponge compressing against cheekbone creating visible skin-depression at point of contact, left hand fingers creating pressure marks on glass bottle, bare feet grounding on hardwood with toe-spread
5. Background motion: Curtain settled from Frame 1 but with residual micro-sway, steam from chai mug in background rising in thin wisp, light shift on wall as golden hour progresses
6. Light in motion: Warm shaft now 5 degrees lower than Frame 1 (time progression), rim light on product bottle creating caustic refraction through amber liquid, subtle golden flicker on vanity surface from curtain-filtered light movement

SPATIAL LOGIC:
- FOREGROUND: Vanity surface with 3-4 products arranged (serum bottle, moisturizer jar closed, cotton pads), slightly out of focus, providing context and depth, occupying bottom 15% of frame
- MIDGROUND: Aira at vanity, sharp focus, hands working on face, primary action and attention plane
- BACKGROUND: Full-length mirror reflecting bedroom behind her (bed with emerald dress still visible), window light source visible in reflection, soft warm bokeh. Bedroom wall with single framed artwork (abstract, warm tones)

LIGHTING:
- Key: Golden hour window light from camera-left, slightly lower angle than Frame 1 (sun descending), medium hardness, 3100K warm
- Fill: Vanity surface bounce from white marble creating under-chin fill at -2.5 stops, soft cool-neutral
- Rim: Hair rim from window at camera-right reflection, thin golden line separating hair from background
- Practical: None
- Light separation: Subject face 1.5 stops brighter than background bedroom

FRAMING: MCU with hands visible — top of head with 6% headroom to below hands at mid-chest level. Subject 65% of frame. Camera height at eye level. Body angle: 3/4 turn, application hand visible on camera-right side of face. Lookroom: standard, breathing space camera-left (where mirror is implied). Crop cuts through mid-forearm on both arms (correct cut point, not at wrist).

LENS: 50mm. APERTURE: f/2.2 — subject sharp, foreground products with gentle blur, background mirror-reflection soft. Warm-tinted bokeh circles.

COMPOSITION REFERENCE: Rule of thirds — Aira's applying hand at right-third vertical, eyes at upper-right intersection. Intimate Bradford Young approach with skin-priority exposure.

ATMOSPHERE: Warm room, golden haze softening edges, intimate proximity feeling, slight humidity from prior shower still in air. Kodak Portra 400 grain.

COLOR GRADE: Warm amber continuing from Frame 1, honey midtones, foundation on skin catching warm highlights, glass bottle refracting amber tones, shadows warm chocolate, lifted blacks. Skin-priority grading — Aira's skin tone is the anchor for all color decisions.

NEGATIVE: mirrored, flipped, inverted, extra limbs, fused fingers, melted features, asymmetric eyes (unintentional), garbled text, floating shadows, duplicated subjects, low-res patches, plastic skin, oversharpened, AI-generated artifacts, watermarks, signature, deformed hands, malformed teeth, joint cuts at ankle/knee/wrist/elbow/neck, amputated fingertips, cross-eyed, lazy eye, off-axis pupils, melted clothing, shoes-not-touching-ground, mismatched footwear pair, mannequin-stiff posture, dead eyes, statue-frozen energy.


### Frame 3 — The Build (Eyes + Through-Mirror Frame)

ASPECT RATIO: 9:16 vertical. SUBJECT: AIRA — Adult woman late 20s-early 30s, South Asian (Indian), warm honey-to-caramel skin tone with golden undertone, 5'6"-5'8", soft-strong hourglass-athletic silhouette, fuller sculpted legs with toned thigh definition, fuller shapely thighs, fuller feminine arms with subtle muscle tone, fuller defined chest in proportion, flat toned midsection, defined waist clear waist-to-hip ratio, curvy hip line with natural feminine flare, heart-shaped to oval face, defined cheekbones, full defined lips with natural cupid's bow, almond-shaped expressive eyes dark brown iris with subtle amber flecks, strong but feminine groomed naturally arched brow, natural sun-kissed glow, long dark brown to near-black hair with subtle warm highlights naturally textured soft waves with body and movement, elegant well-groomed hands.

WARDROBE STATE (Frame 3): Cream silk robe unchanged, both shoulders covered, sash at waist. Fabric draping naturally over seated form.

HAIR STATE (Frame 3): Mostly dry now with defined natural waves forming, still unstyled, no heat tools yet. Pushed back but with face-framing pieces falling forward at both temples. Volume building as hair dries.

MAKEUP STATE (Frame 3 — cumulative): Full base complete (foundation even across entire face, concealer blended under eyes and around nose, setting powder pressed into T-zone). Brows now shaped with pencil (natural arch defined, hair-strokes visible). Eye makeup in progress — transition shade (warm matte brown) blended into crease of right eye completed, left eye being worked on NOW. No liner yet. No mascara yet. Lips still bare with balm. Blush not yet applied. Contour not yet applied.

HAND POSITIONS: Right hand holding fluffy blender brush mid-sweep in left eye crease, pinky braced against left cheekbone for stability, brush angled at 45 degrees with bristles fanning into socket. Left hand holding eyeshadow palette (plum/berry/gold tones visible in pan) at chin height, thumb hooking palette edge, fingers splayed underneath supporting weight, palette tilted toward light so colors readable.

FACIAL MICRO-DYNAMICS: Eyes — left eye slightly closed/squinting for shadow application (lid relaxed for brush access), right eye open and gazing into mirror checking symmetry, asymmetric eye state creating authentic application moment, right eye catchlight at 9 o'clock from mirror-reflected light, amber flecks prominent in open right eye. Brows — newly defined with pencil showing crisp arch, left brow slightly raised from concentration, micro-furrow between brows from precision focus. Lips — pressed together in concentration (lip-press mid-thought), slight tension at corners, thinking-expression, no smile — processing the story internally. Cheeks — foundation smooth and even, natural cheekbone shadow visible without blush/contour yet, apple area neutral in concentration. Jaw — micro-clench of focus, slight tension visible at masseter, chin tucked 5 degrees for mirror-checking angle. Breath — held briefly during precise application, slight chest stillness indicating concentration-breath-hold.

BODY POSTURE: Seated at vanity, leaned 10 degrees forward toward mirror (closer for precision eye work), weight shifted forward onto sitting bones, spine curved forward at upper thoracic, left shoulder slightly raised (arm holding palette elevated), right elbow out and up for brush angle access. Head tilted back 8 degrees and left 5 degrees to expose lid for application.

KINETIC STILLNESS — Six Layers:
1. Subject micro-action: Brush mid-sweep in crease, bristles catching skin creating micro-wake of powder pigment, hand frozen at 60% of blend stroke
2. Fabric/hair state: Robe sleeve fallen to mid-forearm on raised right arm, silk fabric tension visible at shoulder seam from arm elevation, hair strands at temples swaying from head-tilt adjustment, moving right-to-left settling
3. Particulate layer: Micro-particles of eyeshadow powder visible in golden light shaft between palette and face, 4-5 tiny pigment motes floating, catching side-light as warm plum-colored specks
4. Contact-point activity: Brush bristles compressing into lid creating visible skin-flex, pinky pressure-point on cheekbone showing slight skin dimple, palette edge pressing into left thumb pad
5. Background motion: Through-mirror reflection showing bedroom — curtain now still, emerald dress on bed catching shifted light angle, chai steam exhausted (mug cooled), subtle wall shadow shift from lowering golden hour
6. Light in motion: Lower golden angle creating longer shadows across vanity surface, rim-light now wrapping further around right shoulder, catchlight in palette pans shifting as she tilts it, warm flicker on ceiling from fabric-filtered window light

SPATIAL LOGIC:
- FOREGROUND: Camera positioned behind Aira's right shoulder (THROUGH-MIRROR SHOT — most cinematic GRWM angle). Aira's right shoulder and back-of-head visible out of focus in immediate foreground, providing depth and voyeur intimacy. Shoulder silk texture visible but soft.
- MIDGROUND: Aira's REFLECTION in mirror is the sharp-focus primary subject. Her reflected face, hands working, palette visible — all seen through mirror. Mirror frame edges visible creating frame-within-frame.
- BACKGROUND (in reflection): Bedroom behind reflected Aira — vanity surface with products, window light source, warm ambient room visible through her reflection's shoulders.

LIGHTING:
- Key: Golden hour from camera-left (now lower angle, warmer, 3000K), hitting Aira directly AND reflecting in mirror creating doubled light quality
- Fill: Ambient room bounce at -2 stops, warming shadows
- Rim: Edge light on physical Aira's shoulder (foreground) separating her from mirror, bright golden thin line
- Practical: None visible
- Light separation: Mirror-reflected face 1.5 stops brighter than room ambient surrounding mirror frame

FRAMING: Through-mirror composition — camera over Aira's right shoulder shooting into mirror. Physical Aira in soft-focus foreground (shoulder, back of head, arm visible) occupying left 30% of frame. Mirror reflection showing MCU of her face and working hands in sharp focus occupying right 70%. Subject (reflected) at 60% frame height. Headroom in reflection: 10%. Body angle in reflection: frontal, face visible with both hands working.

LENS: 85mm portrait compression — creating intimate shallow depth, compressing the distance between Aira and mirror, beautiful bokeh on foreground shoulder. APERTURE: f/1.8 — razor-thin focus plane on reflection, foreground Aira very soft, background in reflection moderately soft.

COMPOSITION REFERENCE: Frame-within-frame (mirror), Christopher Doyle intimate observational approach, Kubrick symmetry within the mirror reflection while physical frame is asymmetric.

ATMOSPHERE: Deepening golden hour warmth, room feeling more enclosed and intimate as light concentrates, slight warm haze in air, powder particles adding micro-atmosphere near application zone. Kodak Portra 400 grain with slight warmth push.

COLOR GRADE: Amber-gold deepening from Frames 1-2, shadows now warmer (burnt sienna tones), highlights holding golden, plum eyeshadow tones introducing the berry color story that will build through remaining frames. Skin warmth prioritized, slight desaturation on environment to push face forward.

NEGATIVE: mirrored, flipped, inverted, extra limbs, fused fingers, melted features, asymmetric eyes (unintentional), garbled text, floating shadows, duplicated subjects, low-res patches, plastic skin, oversharpened, AI-generated artifacts, watermarks, signature, deformed hands, malformed teeth, joint cuts at ankle/knee/wrist/elbow/neck, amputated fingertips, cross-eyed, lazy eye, off-axis pupils, melted clothing, shoes-not-touching-ground, mismatched footwear pair, mannequin-stiff posture, dead eyes, statue-frozen energy.


### Frame 4 — The Pivot (Lip Color Choice + Decision)

ASPECT RATIO: 9:16 vertical. SUBJECT: AIRA — Adult woman late 20s-early 30s, South Asian (Indian), warm honey-to-caramel skin tone with golden undertone, 5'6"-5'8", soft-strong hourglass-athletic silhouette, fuller sculpted legs with toned thigh definition, fuller shapely thighs, fuller feminine arms with subtle muscle tone, fuller defined chest in proportion, flat toned midsection, defined waist clear waist-to-hip ratio, curvy hip line with natural feminine flare, heart-shaped to oval face, defined cheekbones, full defined lips with natural cupid's bow, almond-shaped expressive eyes dark brown iris with subtle amber flecks, strong but feminine groomed naturally arched brow, natural sun-kissed glow, long dark brown to near-black hair with subtle warm highlights naturally textured soft waves with body and movement, elegant well-groomed hands.

WARDROBE STATE (Frame 4): Cream silk robe now open at front revealing black silk camisole underneath — transition to evening energy beginning. Robe acting as dressing-gown layer, shoulders covered but front revealing the under-layer.

HAIR STATE (Frame 4): Fully dry, now being styled — soft Hollywood waves partially formed. Left side completed (defined S-wave pattern, glossy, voluminous), right side still in natural wave (not yet curled), creating mid-transformation visible asymmetry. Deep side part established on right.

MAKEUP STATE (Frame 4 — cumulative): Full base complete. Brows defined. Full eye look now complete on both eyes (smoked plum crease, deeper outer corner, shimmery champagne lid, blended seamlessly). Eyeliner: thin precise wing on both eyes, extending 3mm past outer corner. Mascara applied — lashes lifted, defined, separated. Contour applied along cheekbones and jawline. Blush swept on apples (warm berry tone). Highlight on cheekbones, brow bone, nose bridge. LIPS: the pivot moment — lip liner in deep berry being applied NOW, cupid's bow being traced, liner defining the shape before color fill.

HAND POSITIONS: Right hand holding lip liner pencil (deep berry shade, wooden pencil with brand name visible on barrel), pencil tip touching upper lip at cupid's bow peak, pinky resting delicately on chin for stability, ring finger curled in. Left hand holding a small compact mirror at jaw height, angled to catch both her lip work and the camera, fingers wrapped around compact's edge, thumb on back.

FACIAL MICRO-DYNAMICS: Eyes — both open and focused downward at compact mirror in left hand, creating a heavy-lidded effect (looking down = lid visible showing completed eye look), lashes fanned and defined casting micro-shadow on upper cheek, slight narrowing suggesting internal decision arriving, catchlight from compact mirror reflection creating secondary light point in lower iris. Brows — right brow raised singular (the knowing expression — the decision moment), left brow steady, creating peak asymmetric expression of the reel, conveying "I know exactly what I'm doing." Lips — mouth slightly open for liner access, upper lip held steady while pencil traces cupid's bow, lower lip relaxed and dropped for access, pre-smile tension building at right corner despite application-open position, liner visible as precise dark berry line on right half of upper lip. Cheeks — blush visible warming the apples, highlight catching on cheekbone with head angle, left cheek slightly pulled from concentration-squint. Jaw — dropped open for lip access but with underlying confidence in the angle, throat exposed and catching golden light, neck tendon visible from head-tilt-back-slightly. Breath — held steady for precision, chest still, shoulders set with quiet confidence.

BODY POSTURE: Still seated but posture transformed — spine straight, shoulders back and open (confidence arriving with the decision), weight centered and grounded. Chin tilted back 10 degrees for compact mirror lip-access angle. Core engaged, subtle postural shift from vulnerable Frame 1 to composed Frame 4.

KINETIC STILLNESS — Six Layers:
1. Subject micro-action: Lip liner pencil mid-stroke at cupid's bow peak, caught at the apex of the defining line, hand frozen mid-precision-draw
2. Fabric/hair state: Left-side Hollywood wave with perfect bounce and shine caught mid-settle after styling, one curl end lifting slightly from residual heat-tool warmth. Robe lapel mid-fall-open revealing camisole, silk sliding. Right-side unstyled hair with natural movement, strand crossing toward face
3. Particulate layer: Golden motes fewer now (sun lower) but concentrated in narrow beam, hair spray micro-mist visible in air from recent left-side styling, catching last golden light
4. Contact-point activity: Pencil tip on lip skin creating micro-indent at cupid's bow, pinky pressing into chin dimple, compact edge pressing into left palm flesh, seated weight pressing into vanity stool
5. Background motion: Bedroom now deeper gold, emerald dress on bed catching last concentrated sun beam, curtain fully still, single jewelry earring on vanity catching light with micro-sparkle from vibration
6. Light in motion: Golden hour near-final stage — concentrated amber beam now narrow and intense, warm wrap on neck and exposed collarbone from camisole reveal, compact mirror bouncing secondary fill upward onto face creating beauty-light effect from below-chin, subtle caustic shimmer on ceiling from compact reflection

SPATIAL LOGIC:
- FOREGROUND: Compact mirror in left hand catching light, slightly soft-focus, reflective surface showing miniature reflection of lips being worked on. Occupies lower-left frame area.
- MIDGROUND: Aira sharp focus, face and working hands as primary action plane, lip liner work as hero detail.
- BACKGROUND: Vanity surface with products (showing progression — used products now open/displaced), mirror reflecting warm bedroom, emerald dress visible in reflection. Soft focus, warm.

LIGHTING:
- Key: Final concentrated golden hour beam from camera-left window, narrow and intense, 2900K deep amber, creating dramatic modeling on face
- Fill: Compact mirror bounce creating upward fill (beauty light effect) on underchin and lower lip area at -1.5 stops from key
- Rim: Strong golden rim on right side of face and hair from concentrated late sun, separating from warm background
- Practical: Compact mirror acting as practical reflector — motivated fill source visible in frame
- Light separation: Face receiving double-light (key + compact bounce) reads 2 stops brighter than background wall

FRAMING: CU — top of head with 5% headroom to collarbone (Beauty Crop variant). Subject 80% of frame. Tighter than previous frames — escalating intimacy at the pivot moment. Camera height: slightly below eye level (looking up at her = confidence angle). Body angle: frontal, face straight-on to camera, hands working at lip level visible. Lookroom: minimal, centered composition for the decision moment.

LENS: 85mm portrait. APERTURE: f/1.8 — ultra-shallow, face razor-sharp, hands slightly soft at near-limit of focus plane, background melted into warm bokeh. Single bokeh circle from earring on vanity.

COMPOSITION REFERENCE: Centered (Wes Anderson conviction), with slight Kubrick symmetry — the moment of decision demands centered framing. Bradford Young skin luminosity approach for the lighting.

ATMOSPHERE: Deep golden concentration, room feeling small and focused, intimate decision-space, hair spray and warmth creating slight soft-focus quality to air. Late Kodak Portra 400 warmth — golden hour approaching final 15 minutes.

COLOR GRADE: Deep amber-gold, berry tones now entering the palette (lip liner introducing the plum/berry thread that matches the eye look and will connect to the emerald dress's jewel-tone register). Shadows warm burnt umber, highlights golden-white, skin glowing with highlight placement visible. Slight film grain increase. Contrast slightly increased for drama at the pivot.

NEGATIVE: mirrored, flipped, inverted, extra limbs, fused fingers, melted features, asymmetric eyes (unintentional), garbled text, floating shadows, duplicated subjects, low-res patches, plastic skin, oversharpened, AI-generated artifacts, watermarks, signature, deformed hands, malformed teeth, joint cuts at ankle/knee/wrist/elbow/neck, amputated fingertips, cross-eyed, lazy eye, off-axis pupils, melted clothing, shoes-not-touching-ground, mismatched footwear pair, mannequin-stiff posture, dead eyes, statue-frozen energy.


### Frame 5 — Near-Complete (Final Touches + Jewelry)

ASPECT RATIO: 9:16 vertical. SUBJECT: AIRA — Adult woman late 20s-early 30s, South Asian (Indian), warm honey-to-caramel skin tone with golden undertone, 5'6"-5'8", soft-strong hourglass-athletic silhouette, fuller sculpted legs with toned thigh definition, fuller shapely thighs, fuller feminine arms with subtle muscle tone, fuller defined chest in proportion, flat toned midsection, defined waist clear waist-to-hip ratio, curvy hip line with natural feminine flare, heart-shaped to oval face, defined cheekbones, full defined lips with natural cupid's bow, almond-shaped expressive eyes dark brown iris with subtle amber flecks, strong but feminine groomed naturally arched brow, natural sun-kissed glow, long dark brown to near-black hair with subtle warm highlights naturally textured soft waves with body and movement, elegant well-groomed hands.

WARDROBE STATE (Frame 5): Robe removed. Now wearing the deep emerald silk slip dress — bias-cut, thin spaghetti straps, fabric skimming body following natural curves, subtle side slit visible at left thigh. # CONCEPT 2 — GRWM

**Concept Line:** "The ritual stays even when the person who gave it meaning leaves."
**Format:** GRWM (Get Ready With Me)
**Stakes:** Getting ready for Karwa Chauth alone this year — the first one without him
**Register:** REVERENT
**Duration:** 56 seconds total
**Frames:** 7 frames x 8 seconds each
**Wardrobe Pillar:** Pillar 4 (Indo-Modern Fusion) — maroon silk modern sari drape with gold blouse, sculpted contemporary pallu, gold border
**Hair:** HC-20 Heritage Crown Braid with maang tikka — center-parted, braided crown wrapping from nape upward, fresh marigold tucked at left temple, maang tikka gold with single pearl drop
**Makeup:** ML-22 Festival Glow — luminous golden base, kohl-defined eyes with soft gold shimmer lid, warm nude lip, highlighted cheekbones with golden warmth, bindi
**Setting:** GRWM Pillar 6 — Indian Heritage (carved wooden vanity, brass tray, heritage textiles BG, diya candlelight, warm tungsten + window light)
**Music:** Contemporary fusion (classical sitar sample + minimal electronic pad), 90 BPM, meditative, slow build
**Opener:** "Suno... pehli baar akeli."
**Sign-off:** Silent (held visual beat — diya flame and sindoor box untouched)
**Voice Mode:** SPOKEN
**Signature Flag:** OPENER-ONLY
**Energy Arc:** Vulnerable (Frame 1) > Processing (Frames 2-3) > Decision/Reverence (Frame 4) > Composure (Frame 5) > Ready (Frame 6) > Exit/Held Silence (Frame 7)

## IMAGE PROMPTS

### Frame 1 — Opening State (Bare Face, Heritage Setting, Stakes)

ASPECT RATIO: 9:16 vertical. SUBJECT: AIRA — Adult woman late 20s-early 30s, South Asian (Indian), warm honey-to-caramel skin tone with golden undertone, 5'6"-5'8", soft-strong hourglass-athletic silhouette, fuller sculpted legs with toned thigh definition, fuller shapely thighs, fuller feminine arms with subtle muscle tone, fuller defined chest in proportion, flat toned midsection, defined waist clear waist-to-hip ratio, curvy hip line with natural feminine flare, heart-shaped to oval face, defined cheekbones, full defined lips with natural cupid's bow, almond-shaped expressive eyes dark brown iris with subtle amber flecks, strong but feminine groomed naturally arched brow, natural sun-kissed glow, long dark brown to near-black hair with subtle warm highlights naturally textured soft waves with body and movement, elegant well-groomed hands.

WARDROBE STATE (Frame 1): Simple cream cotton kurta (collarless, V-neck, loose fit to mid-thigh), bare legs tucked underneath in seated position on floor cushion. Gold bangles stacked on left wrist (everyday pieces, not yet the festival set). Bare feet visible. Hair oil sheen on shoulders of kurta from fresh wash.

HAIR STATE (Frame 1): Freshly washed and oiled, combed straight and damp, center-parted, hanging loose past shoulders, wet-darkened to near-black at ends. No styling, no braiding yet. Natural weight pulling hair flat against back. Slightly frizzy at crown from humidity of recent wash.

MAKEUP STATE (Frame 1): Completely bare. Natural skin with fresh-washed glow, slightly warm from the oil-and-water ritual. No foundation, no concealer. Natural undereye softness visible. Bare brows in natural shape. Bare lips slightly dry. No kohl, no bindi. Clean bare face — the vulnerability of a festival morning before the preparation begins.

HAND POSITIONS: Right hand resting in lap palm-up on cream kurta fabric, relaxed and open, fingers slightly curled, revealing bare ring finger (no ring — the absence speaks). Left hand holding edge of brass thali tray, fingertips touching the rim where traditional items are arranged (kumkum, haldi, diya unlit, sindoor box closed, fresh marigolds).

FACIAL MICRO-DYNAMICS: Eyes — gazing downward at the brass thali in her hand/lap, downcast and contemplative, lashes resting against upper cheek creating soft shadow, slight moisture visible at inner corners (not crying — the wet shine of held emotion), right eye marginally more closed than left (asymmetric contemplation), iris not fully visible due to downcast angle. Brows — inner brow draw (concern/contemplation, slight pull together at center), left brow fractionally higher creating gentle questioning expression, no product so natural brow hairs visible in various directions. Lips — pressed together softly (held emotion), corners neutral-to-slightly-down (not frown, just gravity of feeling), lower lip marginally fuller from the press, slight tremble suggested at left corner. Cheeks — bare and warm from fresh wash, slight natural flush, no contour so full natural face shape visible, cheekbone shadow from downward head tilt. Jaw — soft and slightly dropped, throat-swallow visible (emotion held), neck exposed with wet hair pulled back, tendon visible. Breath — slow and deep, visible shoulder-rise on inhale suggesting gathering-self-before-speaking, chest expanding under loose kurta.

BODY POSTURE: Seated on floor cushion (traditional Indian seating for preparation), legs folded underneath, weight shifted slightly left, spine with natural slight curve forward (not confident-straight yet — vulnerable), shoulders rounded inward (protective, small), head bowed 15 degrees toward the thali. Traditional low-seated intimate posture against carved wooden furniture backdrop.

KINETIC STILLNESS — Six Layers:
1. Subject micro-action: Mid-inhale before speaking, left hand fingers mid-touch settling on brass thali rim, slight weight-shift preparing to look up, the moment before words form
2. Fabric/hair state: Wet hair with single strand separating from mass and falling forward toward face, moving with gravity toward chest, kurta fabric settling from just-sat-down adjustment, cotton creasing at waist fold
3. Particulate layer: Incense smoke from recently-lit agarbatti (sandalwood) rising in thin elegant column from brass holder 40cm to Aira's left, smoke catching warm window light and dispersing into golden threads, 12-15 smoke wisps at various stages of dissipation
4. Contact-point activity: Fingertips on brass thali creating micro-warm-from-metal-contact shine, floor cushion compressing under seated weight with visible fabric tension at edges, wet hair ends leaving slight moisture mark on cream kurta at shoulder
5. Background motion: Diya flame (small clay lamp with cotton wick) on wooden surface flickering with gentle air movement, incense smoke responding to same micro-breeze, dupatta hanging on wall behind with lower edge swaying 2cm from breeze, fresh marigold petals on tray with one petal edge curling from morning air
6. Light in motion: Warm window light from camera-right (early morning east-facing), mixing with warm tungsten from interior creating dual-temp illumination, diya flame creating micro-flicker on nearest brass surface, incense smoke scattering light creating soft god-ray effect in smoke column, window light shaft intensity pulsing with outdoor cloud movement

SPATIAL LOGIC:
- FOREGROUND: Brass thali tray in lap/hand with traditional items visible (kumkum bowl, haldi, closed sindoor box, unlit diya, fresh marigold garland coiled), slightly soft focus at edges, warm brass catching light, occupying lower 25% of frame
- MIDGROUND: Aira seated on embroidered floor cushion, sharp focus, primary subject plane, vulnerable opening posture against heritage backdrop
- BACKGROUND: Heritage setting — carved dark wooden vanity/shelf with ornate mirror (kundan-detail frame), printed dupatta hanging on wall (deep maroon and gold block-print), brass agarbatti holder with smoking incense, small framed photo face-down on shelf (implied narrative — his photo turned away), window with wooden jharokha-style frame showing warm morning light. Soft focus, warm amber tone.

LIGHTING:
- Key: Early morning window light from camera-right (east-facing, 5500K natural mixed with warm interior), medium-soft, creating gentle modeling on face
- Fill: Warm tungsten from heritage brass lamp (out of frame upper-left) at -2 stops, creating golden undertone fill on shadow side
- Rim: Window light edge wrapping around left shoulder where wet hair parts, thin line of morning light separating from background
- Practical: Diya (unlit but present as prop), incense smoke column catching light (atmospheric practical), brass lamp implied warmth
- Light separation: Subject 1.5 stops brighter than background wooden furniture and textile

FRAMING: MCU / Bust — top of head with 8% headroom to mid-chest, cutting through chest area. Subject 72% of frame. Camera height: eye-level (meeting her where she is, not empowering or diminishing). Body angle: 3/4 turn, face angled slightly down and toward thali. Lookroom: downward and toward camera-right where thali draws gaze. Floor-seated composition with slightly elevated camera creating intimate observation angle.

LENS: 50mm. APERTURE: f/2.0 — shallow DOF, subject sharp, foreground thali items soft but recognizable, background heritage setting with warm bokeh circles from brass elements. Warm-tinted bokeh.

COMPOSITION REFERENCE: Bradford Young under-exposed intimacy approach, low-angle wide meeting Spielberg emotional staging, frame-within-frame from ornate mirror visible in background. Golden ratio with Aira's downcast eyes at primary focus intersection.

ATMOSPHERE: Morning ritual quiet, sandalwood incense hanging in air, warm-humid from recent bath, traditional space with lived-in reverence, the heavy lightness of doing something sacred alone for the first time. Kodak 5207 warm with slight grain, lifted shadows.

COLOR GRADE: Warm amber-gold dominant (heritage warmth), deep maroon threading through background textiles (anticipating sari), brass warm-metallic accents, skin tones warm and golden-priority, shadows lifted to warm brown (never cold), slight desaturation creating filmic reverence quality. Earthy, warm, weighted.

NEGATIVE: mirrored, flipped, inverted, extra limbs, fused fingers, melted features, asymmetric eyes (unintentional), garbled text, floating shadows, duplicated subjects, low-res patches, plastic skin, oversharpened, AI-generated artifacts, watermarks, signature, deformed hands, malformed teeth, joint cuts at ankle/knee/wrist/elbow/neck, amputated fingertips, cross-eyed, lazy eye, off-axis pupils, melted clothing, shoes-not-touching-ground, mismatched footwear pair, mannequin-stiff posture, dead eyes, statue-frozen energy.


### Frame 2 — First Application (Skincare + Haldi Ritual Base)

ASPECT RATIO: 9:16 vertical. SUBJECT: AIRA — Adult woman late 20s-early 30s, South Asian (Indian), warm honey-to-caramel skin tone with golden undertone, 5'6"-5'8", soft-strong hourglass-athletic silhouette, fuller sculpted legs with toned thigh definition, fuller shapely thighs, fuller feminine arms with subtle muscle tone, fuller defined chest in proportion, flat toned midsection, defined waist clear waist-to-hip ratio, curvy hip line with natural feminine flare, heart-shaped to oval face, defined cheekbones, full defined lips with natural cupid's bow, almond-shaped expressive eyes dark brown iris with subtle amber flecks, strong but feminine groomed naturally arched brow, natural sun-kissed glow, long dark brown to near-black hair with subtle warm highlights naturally textured soft waves with body and movement, elegant well-groomed hands.

WARDROBE STATE (Frame 2): Same cream cotton kurta, still in floor-seated position on cushion. Bangles pushed up forearm for application access. Slight turmeric-golden stain beginning on fingertips of right hand from haldi application.

HAIR STATE (Frame 2): Still loose and damp-drying, center-parted, now swept behind both ears for face access. Natural wave emerging. No styling yet.

MAKEUP STATE (Frame 2 — cumulative): Moisturizer applied (dewy sheen). Traditional haldi-infused ubtan paste being applied to neck/collarbone area as part of ritual-meets-skincare (golden paste visible on right collarbone). Foundation not yet started — this is the ritual skincare moment. Face dewy from moisturizer only. Brows bare. Lips bare.

HAND POSITIONS: Right hand with fingertips coated in golden haldi paste, mid-application on left collarbone in gentle pressing circles, fingers spread with ring finger and middle finger doing the work. Left hand holding small brass katori (bowl) of golden ubtan paste, cupped in palm with thumb on rim, held at chest height, warm golden paste visible inside.

FACIAL MICRO-DYNAMICS: Eyes — lifted and gazing straight ahead at implied mirror (off-camera), reflective and slightly distant as if remembering, right eye with slight moisture sheen (emotional morning, not tears), catchlight at 2 o'clock from morning window, lashes natural and relaxed, gaze soft-focused not sharp. Brows — relaxed and slightly drawn at inner corners (gentle sadness underlying), natural shape ungroomed, expression of someone lost in thought while hands work automatically. Lips — slightly parted on slow breath, neutral-soft, no smile, lower lip relaxed and full, lip-corner at rest without tension, breath visible as slight lip-movement on inhale. Cheeks — bare and warm, natural flush deepening from the haldi application warmth on skin, cheekbone catching morning light without makeup enhancement. Jaw — soft and relaxed, slight forward set suggesting quiet resolve beneath the vulnerability, throat visible and long. Breath — slow meditative breathing, visible chest expansion, the rhythm of someone in ritual not performance.

BODY POSTURE: Still floor-seated but slightly more upright than Frame 1 — spine straightening as she moves into the doing, shoulders still soft but less rounded, weight now centered. Right arm crossed over body to reach left collarbone creating an intimate self-holding gesture. Slight lean forward.

KINETIC STILLNESS — Six Layers:
1. Subject micro-action: Right fingertips mid-circle on collarbone, pressing golden paste into skin with visible pressure indent, caught mid-rotation of the spreading motion
2. Fabric/hair state: Hair drying and lifting slightly from face, one strand releasing from behind right ear beginning to fall forward, kurta collar shifted from application revealing more collarbone area, cotton fabric at shoulder with slight crease from arm-cross position
3. Particulate layer: Incense smoke continuing (thinner now, 8 minutes elapsed), smoke wisps drifting left across midground, catching morning light at new angle as sun rises, plus micro-particles of golden ubtan paste dust visible near katori bowl catching light
4. Contact-point activity: Fingertip pressure on collarbone creating skin depression and paste-spread visible, brass katori warm in palm with finger indent in paste where she scooped, floor cushion compression unchanged
5. Background motion: Diya still unlit but flame of agarbatti incense flickering, dupatta on wall still, morning light strengthening (slightly brighter shaft through jharokha window), one fresh marigold on thali now with petal fully curled from air-drying
6. Light in motion: Morning light shaft from window now stronger and at marginally different angle (sun rose 3 degrees), golden shaft illuminating the ubtan paste on collarbone creating rich warm highlight on the golden paste against warm skin, brass katori creating small caustic light-bounce on underside of chin

SPATIAL LOGIC:
- FOREGROUND: Brass katori in left hand at lower frame, golden paste visible inside, slightly soft-focus but color-rich, providing cultural context and color story (gold thread beginning)
- MIDGROUND: Aira in application pose, sharp focus, arms crossed-over-body creating intimate self-care geometry, face and collarbone as dual subject plane

### Frame 3 — The Build (Kohl Eyes + Through Mirror)

SUBJECT: AIRA — Adult woman late 20s-early 30s, South Asian (Indian), warm honey-to-caramel skin tone with golden undertone, 5'6"-5'8", soft-strong hourglass-athletic silhouette, fuller sculpted legs with toned thigh definition, fuller shapely thighs, fuller feminine arms with subtle muscle tone, fuller defined chest in proportion, flat toned midsection, defined waist clear waist-to-hip ratio, curvy hip line with natural feminine flare, heart-shaped to oval face, defined cheekbones, full defined lips with natural cupid's bow, almond-shaped expressive eyes dark brown iris with subtle amber flecks, strong but feminine groomed naturally arched brow, natural sun-kissed glow, long dark brown to near-black hair with subtle warm highlights naturally textured soft waves with body and movement, elegant well-groomed hands.

WARDROBE STATE (Frame 3): Still in cream kurta, but gold blouse (for sari) now visible on carved wooden hanger behind her in heritage mirror reflection — the outfit waiting.

HAIR STATE (Frame 3): Now dry, center-parted, beginning of braid formation — front sections braided at temples creating the start of the heritage crown braid, back still loose. Transitional state.

MAKEUP STATE (Frame 3 — cumulative): Base foundation now applied (luminous golden finish, dewy). Concealer blended. No contour yet. Brows defined with pencil in natural arch. KOHL being applied NOW — traditional kajal pencil on lower waterline of left eye, right eye already complete (dark kohl-rimmed lower and upper waterline, smudged slightly for softness). Gold shimmer eyeshadow pressed on lids (both eyes). No lip color yet. No blush yet. No bindi yet.

HAND POSITIONS: Right hand holding traditional kajal pencil (thick wooden kohl pencil, darkened tip), drawing along lower waterline of left eye with pencil angled inward, pinky and ring finger resting on left cheekbone for stability. Left hand gently pulling lower left eyelid down at outer corner to create taut surface for application, fingertip at outer eye corner.

FACIAL MICRO-DYNAMICS: Eyes — left eye held open wide for kohl application (lower waterline exposed), slight watering of left eye from pencil contact creating authentic application-tear, right eye already kohl-rimmed looking darker and more defined than left (mid-application asymmetry), gaze directed at own reflection in ornate heritage mirror, concentration and care visible. Brows — left brow lifted to help hold eye open for application, right brow relaxed creating application-asymmetry, defined with pencil now showing cleaner arch than bare Frame 1. Lips — pressed together in application concentration, slight tension at corners from holding still, breathing through nose (lips closed to minimize facial movement during eye work). Cheeks — golden base now smooth and luminous, cheekbone catching light without blush/highlight yet, slight tension at left cheek from eye-pulling gesture. Jaw — set and steady for precision work, micro-tension at masseter from concentration, chin slightly tucked. Breath — held briefly for precision, visible subtle chest-stillness.

BODY POSTURE: Now seated slightly higher — moved from floor cushion to low wooden stool (traditional carved) for mirror access. Spine straighter than Frames 1-2 (confidence building through ritual progression). Leaned forward 10 degrees toward mirror for precision. Right elbow out for pencil access, left arm crossed over to assist.

KINETIC STILLNESS — Six Layers:
1. Subject micro-action: Kohl pencil mid-draw along waterline, tip in contact with pink tissue creating dark line, caught at 50% of the lower-lid stroke, hands frozen in precision hold

3. Particulate layer: Incense now fully burnt out but residual smoke haze lingering at ceiling level diffusing light, fine kohl pencil dust visible in close proximity to eye area (2-3 micro-particles in key-light beam), morning light dust motes in background shaft
4. Contact-point activity: Kohl tip pressing into waterline creating slight tissue depression, left fingertip pulling skin taut at outer eye corner creating visible skin-stretch, body weight pressing into carved wooden stool seat
5. Background motion: Heritage mirror reflecting warm room behind Aira (we see this through camera-over-shoulder THROUGH-MIRROR composition), gold blouse on hanger swaying micro-movement from earlier passage, diya still present on shelf (still unlit), morning light now fully established creating stable warm environment
6. Light in motion: Morning light now full and stable from camera-right, golden fill from brass lamp creating warm shadow-side tone, mirror reflection creating secondary light-bounce into Aira's face acting as unintentional beauty fill, slight caustic pattern on ceiling from brass tray reflection

- MIDGROUND: Aira's REFLECTION in ornate heritage mirror — sharp focus, face and kohl-applying hands visible in reflection. Kundan-detailed mirror frame creating ornate frame-within-frame with traditional craftsmanship visible in gold and glass inlay.

### Frame 4 — The Pivot (Braid + Maang Tikka)

ASPECT RATIO: 9:16 vertical. SUBJECT: AIRA — Adult woman late 20s-early 30s, South Asian (Indian), warm honey-to-caramel skin tone with golden undertone, 5'6"-5'8", soft-strong hourglass-athletic silhouette, fuller sculpted legs with toned thigh definition, fuller shapely thighs, fuller feminine arms with subtle muscle tone, fuller defined chest in proportion, flat toned midsection, defined waist clear waist-to-hip ratio, curvy hip line with natural feminine flare, heart-shaped to oval face, defined cheekbones, full defined lips with natural cupid's bow, almond-shaped expressive eyes dark brown iris with subtle amber flecks, strong but feminine groomed naturally arched brow, natural sun-kissed glow, long dark brown to near-black hair with subtle warm highlights naturally textured soft waves with body and movement, elegant well-groomed hands.

WARDROBE STATE (Frame 4): Cream kurta with gold blouse now layered underneath (visible at neckline — gold fabric edge showing at collar, transitioning toward final look). Hair being worked on as main event.

HAIR STATE (Frame 4): Heritage crown braid NOW being completed — both sides braided from temples and meeting at crown in an elegant woven crown formation, being pinned into place with gold hairpins. Back section gathered into low sculptural bun at nape. Maang tikka being placed NOW — gold with single pearl drop, hooking into center part at forehead. Fresh marigold sprig being tucked at left temple alongside the braid. Mid-styling kinetic moment.

MAKEUP STATE (Frame 4 — cumulative): Full base. Kohl complete (both eyes, smudged beautifully). Gold shimmer lids complete. Brows defined. Contour now applied (cheekbones sculpted). Blush applied (warm peach-gold tone on apples). Highlight on cheekbones. No lip color yet. No bindi yet.

HAND POSITIONS: Right hand at hairline placing maang tikka hook into center-part hair, fingertips delicately positioning the gold chain and pearl pendant, thumb and index finger working the small hook mechanism. Left hand holding a gold hairpin at crown level, about to secure the braid junction, pin held between index and middle finger ready to insert.

FACIAL MICRO-DYNAMICS: Eyes — gazing upward at mirror (arms are up, so eyes track upward to see hair work), upward gaze revealing full kohl-rimmed beauty of completed eye look, slight softening of gaze suggesting the weight of the moment (putting on the tikka she used to have him place), catchlight high in iris from upward gaze at 12 o'clock, amber flecks prominent in direct light. Brows — raised both slightly for the upward mirror-check, creating slight forehead lines visible (real, human, unfiltered), gentle concerned expression beneath the practical upward gaze. Lips — softly parted, breath flowing, slight downturn at corners not from sadness but from the weight of memory, lower lip relaxed and full, pre-speech tremble as if she might say something but doesn't. Cheeks — contour now sculpting the cheekbones visibly, blush warming the apples, highlight catching from upward-tilted head angle. Jaw — elongated from head-tilt-back for tikka placement access, throat long and exposed, slight swallow-pulse visible at base of throat. Breath — arms-up position requiring deeper breath, visible ribcage expansion, slight tremble in exhale.

BODY POSTURE: Seated on carved stool, spine straight and elongated (arms raised forces good posture), both arms elevated for hair work creating elegant shoulder-collarbone-arm triangle, head tilted back slightly for tikka access at hairline. Weight centered, core engaged to hold pose, slight arch in lower back from arms-up position.

KINETIC STILLNESS — Six Layers:
1. Subject micro-action: Right fingertips mid-hook of maang tikka into hair part, pearl pendant swinging with micro-pendulum motion from the positioning, left hand with pin about to insert, the mechanical precision of sacred adornment
2. Fabric/hair state: Crown braid with individual braided strands visible and catching light, loose baby hairs at nape catching breeze and light, marigold sprig at left temple with petals slightly disturbed from insertion, kurta sleeve falling to mid-upper-arm from raised position revealing toned arm
3. Particulate layer: Fresh marigold fragrance suggested through micro-pollen particles visible in light near the flower, morning light catching fine hair-fly-aways at crown creating golden halo effect, 6-8 luminous micro-particles
4. Contact-point activity: Tikka hook pressing into hair part with visible hair displacement, hairpin point about to enter braid junction creating pre-contact tension, seated weight on stool creating wood-creak suggestion, bare toes curled on floor
5. Background motion: Heritage mirror reflecting the back of Aira's braided head (viewer gets both front view and back-of-head in mirror simultaneously), morning light fully established and stable, single remaining incense stick smoke-trail thin and vertical (still air)
6. Light in motion: Morning sun now direct and warm through jharokha window creating geometric light pattern on far wall, maang tikka gold catching and refracting morning beam creating tiny starburst at pendant, gold hairpins creating point-sparkle array at crown, pearl pendant with internal glow from transmitted light

SPATIAL LOGIC:
- FOREGROUND: Fresh marigold in extreme soft focus at left edge of frame (from the sprig being placed), orange-gold petals large and close, providing color and cultural context in immediate foreground
- MIDGROUND: Aira with arms raised working on crown braid and tikka, sharp focus on face and hands at crown, primary action at head level
- BACKGROUND: Heritage room — ornate mirror now showing back-of-head braid work (functional and compositional), carved wooden shelf with brass items, warm wall with dupatta, morning-lit atmosphere. Warm soft focus.

LIGHTING:
- Key: Full morning window from camera-right, now direct sun 5000K, medium-hard creating defined shadows on raised arms and face from arm-shadow interplay
- Fill: Brass lamp warm from camera-left at -2 stops, golden fill on shadow areas
- Rim: Morning light wrapping around raised arms creating bright edge-definition against background, arm skin glowing with rim
- Practical: Gold jewelry (tikka, pins) acting as micro-practical light sources — catching and redistributing key light
- Light separation: Arms and face 1.5+ stops brighter than background furniture

FRAMING: MS / Waist — top of raised hands (above head) with 3% headroom to waist level. Subject 70% of frame. Camera height: eye level (meeting the elevated work). Body angle: frontal, face tilted back revealing under-chin and throat, arms up creating visual triangle with head as apex. Lookroom: centered for this symmetrical ritual moment.

LENS: 50mm. APERTURE: f/2.0 — focus on face and tikka-placement hands, foreground marigold very soft, background heritage room soft with warm circular bokeh.

COMPOSITION REFERENCE: Centered symmetry (the sacred moment demands center-frame reverence), slight Kubrick precision, Emmanuel Lubezki morning-light celebration. Arms creating triangular frame with head at center.

## VIDEO PROMPTS

### Frame 1 — Video (Opening State)

SHOT TYPE: MCU / Bust. CAMERA MOVEMENT: Static with micro breathing drift (gimbal-smooth, imperceptible sway simulating intimate proximity, 1mm total movement). LENS: 50mm. SUBJECT ACTION: Aira seated on floor cushion in cream kurta, right hand resting in lap palm-up (bare ring finger visible), left hand touching brass thali rim. Slow inhale with shoulder-rise at 0.0-1.0s, then eyes lift from downcast-at-thali to camera at 1.0s mark, opener line begins at 1.2s. After VO delivery, eyes return to thali with slow blink at 6.0s, slight finger-curl on right hand in lap. LIGHTING: Morning window from right (east-facing, 5500K mixed warm), incense smoke column rising catching light, brass lamp warm fill from left, heritage setting ambiance. ENVIRONMENT + ATMOSPHERE: Heritage GRWM setting — carved wooden furniture, ornate mirror, incense smoking, brass thali in lap with kumkum/haldi/diya/marigolds, maroon dupatta on wall, jharokha window, warm humid morning air. AUDIO: Music at -24dB (sitar sample, single note sustained, minimal electronic pad beneath, 90 BPM — barely present, meditative), ambient (incense sizzle faint, fabric rustle, morning birds outside window very distant), VO [AIRA, reverent register, low and breath-forward, 120 wpm slow-deliberate]: "Suno... pehli baar akeli." — delivery: "Suno" as intimate command-whisper with 0.4s breath before, ellipsis pause 0.8s (eyes track from thali to camera during this pause), "pehli baar" with weight on each word equally, "akeli" dropped lower in pitch on final syllable with slight throat-catch, final word hanging in air. DURATION: 8 seconds. FRAME RATE: 24fps. MOTION BLUR: 180-degree shutter, minimal motion (still subject), incense smoke flowing naturally. LIP-SYNC: Hindi throughout — "Suno" open round mouth shape, pause, "pehli" with lip-pursed P, "baar" open, "akeli" with open A and L tongue-touch. TEMPORAL LOGIC: 0.0-1.0s inhale and shoulder-rise, 1.0-1.2s eyes lift to camera, 1.2-6.0s VO delivery with held stillness, 6.0-7.5s eyes return downward with slow blink, 7.5-8.0s held still beat with breath.

NEGATIVE: morphing, warping, identity drift, limb teleport, object pop-in, frame skip, mirrored composition, text overlay, watermark, AI artifact, ghosting, double exposure unless intended, lip-sync drift, audio desync, wardrobe drift between shots, unmotivated camera shake, physics violation (water/fire/hair/fabric), mannequin posture, frozen background, identity flicker.

### Frame 2 — Video (First Application)

SHOT TYPE: MCU with hands/collarbone visible. CAMERA MOVEMENT: Slow tilt down (from face to collarbone over 3 seconds, then static hold showing haldi application, 5-second hold, slight return tilt-up in final 1s). LENS: 50mm. SUBJECT ACTION: Aira applying haldi ubtan paste to collarbone — right hand with golden paste on fingertips making gentle circles on left collarbone, left hand holding brass katori of paste at chest height. At 5.0s, slight pause in application, fingertips rest on collarbone, brief glance down at hands as if registering the ritual, then resumes. LIGHTING: Morning window strengthening from right, ubtan paste catching golden light on collarbone, brass katori warm reflections, warm ambient fill. ENVIRONMENT + ATMOSPHERE: Heritage setting continuity, incense smoke thinner, morning light strengthening through jharokha, warm meditative rhythm, ritual-skincare atmosphere. AUDIO: Music at -18dB (sitar developing melody slowly, electronic pad evolving, tabla pattern beginning very subtle at 90 BPM), ambient (paste-on-skin soft sound, katori metal-on-palm, breath), VO [AIRA, reverent continuing, 130 wpm]: "Har saal, woh ready hota tha saath mein..." slight breath "...getting ready was never this quiet." — delivery: Hindi opening "Har saal" with nostalgic softening, "woh ready hota tha saath mein" natural Hindi flow with slight ache, breath-pause bridging to English, English portion slightly faster and more matter-of-fact, "quiet" as final word fading to near-whisper. DURATION: 8 seconds. FRAME RATE: 24fps. MOTION BLUR: 180-degree shutter, hand circles creating soft motion arc on collarbone, natural gentle movement. LIP-SYNC: Hindi opening transitioning to English, natural bilingual flow, lips matching phonemes in both languages. TEMPORAL LOGIC: 0.0-3.0s tilt-down with continuous application, 3.0-5.0s static hold on collarbone application, 5.0-5.5s pause and downward glance, 5.5-7.0s resumes with slight return tilt, 7.0-8.0s settled continuation.

NEGATIVE: morphing, warping, identity drift, limb teleport, object pop-in, frame skip, mirrored composition, text overlay, watermark, AI artifact, ghosting, double exposure unless intended, lip-sync drift, audio desync, wardrobe drift between shots, unmotivated camera shake, physics violation (water/fire/hair/fabric), mannequin posture, frozen background, identity flicker.

### Frame 3 — Video (Through Mirror — Kohl)

SHOT TYPE: OTS through-mirror. CAMERA MOVEMENT: Parallax slide left-to-right (slow 4cm truck over 8 seconds, shifting the foreground/reflection relationship, revealing more of mirror reflection progressively). LENS: 85mm. SUBJECT ACTION: Viewed through mirror — Aira applying kohl to lower waterline. Right hand holding kajal pencil drawing along lower lid, left hand pulling lower lid taut at outer corner. Precision and concentration visible. At 4.0s, completes left eye, sets pencil down, looks at reflection directly with both kohl-rimmed eyes, brief pause of self-recognition, slight nod to self. LIGHTING: Through-mirror — morning light from right visible in mirror as light source, edge-light on physical shoulder (foreground), reflected face warmly lit, kohl pencil dust particles visible in light beam near face. ENVIRONMENT + ATMOSPHERE: Heritage mirror with kundan frame creating ornate frame-within-frame, room reflected behind Aira showing gold blouse on hanger (anticipation), warm morning interior, precision ritual atmosphere. AUDIO: Music at -18dB (sitar melody developing, tabla clearer now, electronic bed sustained, 90 BPM building), ambient (pencil-on-skin faint, breath held then released, blink-after-application), VO [AIRA, contemplative deepening, 125 wpm]: "Mujhe yaad hai... the way he used to watch me get ready." pause "That look." pause "Maine socha tha it was forever." — delivery: "Mujhe yaad hai" soft and internal (Hindi memory-phrase), English switch "the way he used to watch" with slight rising inflection on "watch," single-beat pause, "That look" dropped and weighted, longer 0.6s pause, "Maine socha tha it was forever" with Hindi-English blend spoken as unified thought, "forever" final word landing heavy. DURATION: 8 seconds. FRAME RATE: 24fps. MOTION BLUR: 180-degree shutter, parallax creating gentle foreground/background shift, pencil strokes minimal blur, natural breathing movement. LIP-SYNC: Through mirror-reflection — ensure lip movements match reflected (correct mirror orientation), Hindi/English bilingual flow. TEMPORAL LOGIC: 0.0-4.0s kohl application with parallax developing, 4.0-4.5s pencil set-down, 4.5-5.0s self-recognition pause with direct mirror-gaze, 5.0-7.5s VO delivery, 7.5-8.0s slight nod and settle.

### Frame 7 — Video (Exit Beat — Diya + Silence)

SHOT TYPE: CU transitioning to ECU. CAMERA MOVEMENT: Slow push-in (from CU showing face and hands with diya to ECU on diya flame + sindoor box at end, 8 seconds, creeping attention toward the narrative detail). LENS: 50mm to macro-equivalent through proximity. At 5.0s camera drifts downward — her hand withdraws past the CLOSED sindoor box without touching it. Final 3 seconds: ECU on lit diya flame beside untouched sindoor box — Aira's fingertips visible at frame edge withdrawing, the narrative absence complete. LIGHTING: Match-strike creating flash, then flame-glow as primary warm practical on face (2200K dancing orange-gold), morning light as secondary fill from right, the interplay of stable daylight and flickering flame creating dynamic face-illumination, final ECU lit entirely by diya flame on brass-and-red objects. ENVIRONMENT + ATMOSPHERE: Intimate heritage shelf corner, brass surfaces catching flame, the sacred-private space, smoke from extinguished match mixing with diya smoke, warm still air, profound silence and weight. AUDIO: Music drops to -24dB at 0.0s (near-silence, single sustained sitar note holding), ambient (match-strike sharp at 0.5s, flame-catch whisper at 2.0s, diya-flame crackle micro-sound, breath — slow exhale at 4.0s, ambient quiet), VO: SILENT. The sign-off is silence. No words. The unlit sindoor and lit diya tell the entire story. Final 2s: music fades completely to pure ambient (diya flame, distant morning birds, one deep breath). DURATION: 8 seconds. FRAME RATE: 24fps. MOTION BLUR: 180-degree shutter, match-strike creating brief flash-blur, flame-flicker as constant micro-motion, push-in smooth and inexorable toward the narrative detail. LIP-SYNC: No speech. Lips visible in opening CU — closed, soft, held emotion. TEMPORAL LOGIC: 0.0-0.5s match strike, 0.5-2.0s match held above wick (pause, breath), 2.0-2.5s flame-to-wick transfer (diya ignites), 2.5-4.0s face in flame-glow watching, 4.0-5.0s match set down, hand withdraws, 5.0-8.0s camera pushes to ECU on lit diya + closed sindoor box, hand exiting frame.
