# CONCEPT 3 — GRWM

**Concept Line:** "Armor isn't metal — it's a red lip and a spine that refuses to bend."
**Format:** GRWM (Get Ready With Me)
**Stakes:** Getting ready for the brand event where everyone will judge whether I belong
**Register:** ELECTRIC
**Duration:** 48 seconds total
**Frames:** 6 frames x 8 seconds each
**Wardrobe Pillar:** Pillar 2 (Editorial Bold) — crimson sculptural one-shoulder gown, architectural draped shoulder creating asymmetric volume, floor-length column silhouette
**Hair:** HC-11 Wet-Look High Pony — slicked back tightly from face, high ponytail with wet-gel finish, sleek and sharp
**Makeup:** ML-13 Graphic Liner — sharp black graphic wing extending past outer corner, clean matte skin, bold brow, bare lip initially building to deep red
**Setting:** GRWM Pillar 4 — Mirror-Wall Studio (full mirrored wall, polished concrete floor, single hard magenta key light, clean haze, controlled negative space)
**Music:** Synth-bold drums-driven, 120 BPM, confident, sharp, building intensity
**Opener:** "Dekho, they said I shouldn't be there."
**Sign-off:** "Watch me."
**Voice Mode:** SPOKEN
**Signature Flag:** FULL
**Energy Arc:** Vulnerable (Frame 1) > Processing/Building (Frames 2-3) > Decision/Defiance (Frame 4) > Electric (Frame 5) > Loose/Powerful (Frame 6)

## IMAGE PROMPTS

### Frame 1 — Opening State

ASPECT RATIO: 9:16 vertical. SUBJECT: AIRA — Adult woman late 20s-early 30s, South Asian (Indian), warm honey-to-caramel skin tone with golden undertone, 5'6"-5'8", soft-strong hourglass-athletic silhouette, fuller sculpted legs with toned thigh definition, fuller shapely thighs, fuller feminine arms with subtle muscle tone, fuller defined chest in proportion, flat toned midsection, defined waist clear waist-to-hip ratio, curvy hip line with natural feminine flare, heart-shaped to oval face, defined cheekbones, full defined lips with natural cupid's bow, almond-shaped expressive eyes dark brown iris with subtle amber flecks, strong but feminine groomed naturally arched brow, natural sun-kissed glow, long dark brown to near-black hair with subtle warm highlights naturally textured soft waves with body and movement, elegant well-groomed hands.

WARDROBE STATE (Frame 1): Black silk robe with satin sheen, knee-length, tied at waist, minimal and editorial. Bare legs visible, bare feet on polished concrete floor. Studio preparation state.

HAIR STATE (Frame 1): Loose and natural, recently washed, slightly damp, no product yet. Hanging past shoulders in natural waves. Pre-styling state before the slick-back will happen.

MAKEUP STATE (Frame 1): Bare face — completely clean. Skin slightly matte from recent cleanse (no moisturizer sheen yet). No foundation, no concealer, no color anywhere. Natural undereye visible. Bare brows. Bare lips. The editorial blank canvas.

HAND POSITIONS: Right hand gripping edge of styling chair back, knuckles visible with slight tension (nerves), standing behind the chair using it as anchor. Left hand at side of neck, fingertips touching below left ear in a self-soothing hold (the gesture of someone processing anxiety).

FACIAL MICRO-DYNAMICS: Eyes — direct challenging gaze at camera/mirror-wall (the full mirrored wall reflects her entire body back), eyes slightly widened in the vulnerable moment before defiance arrives, dark brown with amber flecks catching the magenta studio key, catchlight at 2 o'clock from hard key light, slight moisture at inner corners (adrenaline, not tears), lower lids with micro-tension from intensity building. Brows — slightly drawn together at center (concern transitioning to determination), natural ungroomed shape, left brow fractionally lower (the skeptical challenge forming). Lips — pressed together with visible jaw-muscle engagement, corners slightly downturned in concentration/determination, lower lip caught between teeth briefly (the nervous-to-brave transition), no color so natural pink-brown tone visible. Cheeks — bare, angular studio lighting creating dramatic shadow beneath cheekbone, no makeup so bone structure creating its own drama. Jaw — set forward slightly (defiance building), visible masseter tension, chin lifted 5 degrees (the first physical signal of "I'm going"), throat pulse visible. Breath — held mid-inhale, chest expanded, the breath before a declaration.

BODY POSTURE: Standing behind styling chair, using it as physical barrier/anchor, weight on left leg with right hip cocked, spine straight but shoulders with slight protective curl forward (not yet open-confident), head lifted (the early sign of defiance), barefoot grounding on cold concrete. The posture between vulnerability and armor.

KINETIC STILLNESS — Six Layers:
1. Subject micro-action: Right hand grip tightening on chair back (knuckle-white beginning), left hand fingertips pressing into neck flesh below ear (self-holding), weight shifting forward onto balls of feet as if about to step into something
2. Fabric/hair state: Black silk robe with one lapel slightly open from the neck-touch gesture, satin catching magenta key light with liquid reflection, hair with one strand falling forward past shoulder caught mid-sway from the head-lift
3. Particulate layer: Clean theatrical haze in studio — thin even fog catching magenta key light creating pink-tinted atmosphere throughout the space, 20+ subtle haze particles visible in light beam, creating depth
4. Contact-point activity: Knuckles pressing into chair-back chrome creating flesh-compression at grip, fingertips pressing into neck skin below ear creating micro-indent, bare feet flat on cold polished concrete with toe-spread for stability
5. Background motion: Mirror-wall reflecting entire studio space including Aira from behind (dual view), clean haze drifting slowly left-to-right in magenta light beam, styling chair on wheels with micro-vibration from her grip
6. Light in motion: Single hard magenta key from camera-left at 45 degrees creating dramatic split-light on face (one side magenta-lit, other in shadow), light beam visible in haze creating volumetric magenta shaft, edge of light cutting sharply across concrete floor

SPATIAL LOGIC:
- FOREGROUND: Styling chair back (chrome and black leather) in lower 20% of frame, slightly out of focus, Aira's grip on it visible as connection point
- MIDGROUND: Aira standing, sharp focus, primary subject against mirror-wall, dramatic single-light studio setup
- BACKGROUND: Full mirror-wall reflecting the studio — Aira's full body from behind visible in reflection (showing bare legs, robe, loose hair from reverse angle), magenta light source visible in reflection as bright point, polished floor reflecting, empty studio negative space. Clean and controlled.

LIGHTING:
- Key: Single hard magenta gel key from camera-left at 45 degrees, high position (above head), creating dramatic Rembrandt triangle on face with magenta color cast, hard shadow edge
- Fill: Minimal — ambient from mirror-wall bounce only at -3 stops, creating deep shadows on right side of face
- Rim: Mirror-wall reflection creating subtle rear-bounce on back of shoulders, cool-neutral against magenta key
- Practical: None — studio stripped to single light for maximum drama
- Light separation: Subject 2+ stops brighter than background (magenta key concentrating on her, background in deep shadow with only haze-glow)

FRAMING: MCU / Bust — top of head with 8% headroom to mid-chest. Subject 75% of frame. Camera height: eye level, direct confrontation. Body angle: frontal, direct, challenging. Lookroom: minimal — centered composition for direct-address intensity. The mirror-wall creates infinite-depth behind her.

LENS: 50mm. APERTURE: f/2.0 — subject sharp, chair foreground slightly soft, mirror-wall reflection soft at depth creating infinite-regression feeling. Bokeh tinted magenta from key light color.

COMPOSITION REFERENCE: Fincher locked-off precision (symmetrical confrontation), split-lighting drama (Caravaggio chiaroscuro with modern magenta update), negative space dominant.

ATMOSPHERE: Editorial studio, controlled and intentional, the solitude of preparation before performance, magenta-dramatic single-light creating fashion-editorial mood, clean haze adding depth without clutter, the calm before the storm. High-contrast fashion film quality.

COLOR GRADE: High contrast — magenta key creating warm-pink highlights on lit side, deep shadow on unlit side, polished concrete cool-neutral at floor, black robe absorbing light, skin catching magenta warmth. Desaturated overall except for the magenta key color. Crushed blacks at edges. Editorial film grade.

NEGATIVE: mirrored, flipped, inverted, extra limbs, fused fingers, melted features, asymmetric eyes (unintentional), garbled text, floating shadows, duplicated subjects, low-res patches, plastic skin, oversharpened, AI-generated artifacts, watermarks, signature, deformed hands, malformed teeth, joint cuts at ankle/knee/wrist/elbow/neck, amputated fingertips, cross-eyed, lazy eye, off-axis pupils, melted clothing, shoes-not-touching-ground, mismatched footwear pair, mannequin-stiff posture, dead eyes, statue-frozen energy.

## VIDEO PROMPTS

### Frame 1 — Video (Opening State)

SHOT TYPE: MCU / Bust. CAMERA MOVEMENT: Static locked-off (Fincher precision, zero movement, confrontational stillness for 8 seconds). LENS: 50mm. SUBJECT ACTION: Aira standing behind styling chair, gripping edge. At 0.0-1.0s, slow inhale with visible shoulder-rise and jaw-set. At 1.2s, eyes snap to camera and opener VO begins. Hands remain gripping chair throughout (the tension anchor). At 5.5s, right hand releases chair — fingers unfurl deliberately. Slight chin-lift at 7.0s as the defiance settles. LIGHTING: Single hard magenta key from camera-left, dramatic split-light, deep shadows, clean studio haze catching beam. ENVIRONMENT + ATMOSPHERE: Mirror-Wall Studio — polished concrete, full mirrored wall, clean haze, single hard light, editorial stripped-down space. AUDIO: Music enters at 0.0s at -18dB (synth pad, single tension chord held, 120 BPM kick drum pattern emerging), ambient (studio hum, breath), VO [AIRA, electric register, 155 wpm, crisp and clipped]: "Dekho, they said I shouldn't be there." pause 0.4s "So." — delivery: "Dekho" sharp with direct eye-contact lock (Hindi commanding attention), rapid "they said I shouldn't be there" as single breath-group with building energy, pause, "So." dropped lower as single syllable carrying all the weight and implication. DURATION: 8 seconds. FRAME RATE: 24fps. MOTION BLUR: 180-degree shutter, minimal motion (mostly static subject), subtle haze drift. LIP-SYNC: Hindi "Dekho" opening then English — crisp articulation matching electric register. TEMPORAL LOGIC: 0.0-1.0s inhale and tension build, 1.0-1.2s eyes snap to camera, 1.2-5.0s VO delivery, 5.0-5.5s hand-release from chair, 5.5-7.0s held beat, 7.0-8.0s chin-lift settle.

NEGATIVE: morphing, warping, identity drift, limb teleport, object pop-in, frame skip, mirrored composition, text overlay, watermark, AI artifact, ghosting, double exposure unless intended, lip-sync drift, audio desync, wardrobe drift between shots, unmotivated camera shake, physics violation (water/fire/hair/fabric), mannequin posture, frozen background, identity flicker.

### Frame 2 — Video (First Application)

SHOT TYPE: MCU with hands. CAMERA MOVEMENT: Slow push-in (imperceptible, 1.5cm over 8 seconds, building intensity through proximity). LENS: 50mm. SUBJECT ACTION: Aira in styling chair, right hand stippling foundation with kabuki brush across cheek, left hand holding pump bottle. Rhythmic stipple pattern visible. At 3.0s, brief pause to pump more product. At 4.5s, resumes with increased intensity (faster stipple). Eyes maintain mirror-focus throughout with occasional snap-to-camera at 2.0s and 6.0s. LIGHTING: Magenta key continuity, brush-motion casting moving shadows. ENVIRONMENT + ATMOSPHERE: Studio setting, chair, tools visible in mirror reflection, haze continuing. AUDIO: Music at -14dB (synth building, kick drum clearer, snare entering, 120 BPM establishing), ambient (brush-on-skin whisper sound, product pump click at 3.0s), VO [AIRA, electric building, 160 wpm]: "Main jaanti hoon how they look at me." quick breath "Like I need to earn the room." slight laugh-scoff "Please." — delivery: Hindi "Main jaanti hoon" (I know) with weighted knowing, immediate English switch "how they look at me" faster and matter-of-fact, breath, "Like I need to earn the room" with slight bitter edge rising, scoff-laugh, "Please" as single dismissive syllable dropped low with eyeroll energy. DURATION: 8 seconds. FRAME RATE: 24fps. MOTION BLUR: 180-degree shutter, brush-stipple creating rhythmic motion blur arc, push-in smooth. LIP-SYNC: Hindi/English bilingual flow, lips matching both languages naturally, slight lip-press between thoughts. TEMPORAL LOGIC: 0.0-3.0s steady application with VO beginning, 3.0-3.5s pump-pause, 3.5-7.0s resumed application with VO continuing, 7.0-8.0s held beat with settled brush.

NEGATIVE: morphing, warping, identity drift, limb teleport, object pop-in, frame skip, mirrored composition, text overlay, watermark, AI artifact, ghosting, double exposure unless intended, lip-sync drift, audio desync, wardrobe drift between shots, unmotivated camera shake, physics violation (water/fire/hair/fabric), mannequin posture, frozen background, identity flicker.

LIP-SYNC: English only, crisp consonants per electric register, lips visible between hair/liner work. ### Frame 4 — Video (The Pivot — Red Lip)

SHOT TYPE: ECU to CU. CAMERA MOVEMENT: Slow pull-back (from ECU on lips to CU showing full face over 8 seconds — beginning micro-focused on lip application then revealing the full powerful face as red lip completes). LENS: 85mm macro-capable. SUBJECT ACTION: Opens at ECU — lipstick bullet touching lower lip, single decisive swipe from center to corner in first 2 seconds (hero stroke). At 2.5s lips close together (blot-press distributing color). Camera begins pull-back. At 4.0s full face visible with complete red lip — slight lip-press-pop to settle color. At 5.0s delivers pivot VO line with direct camera-stare and single raised brow. At 7.0s, capped lipstick set down deliberately (finality click). LIGHTING: Magenta key creating maximum saturation on crimson lip (the color reads vivid and intense), graphic liner visible in pull-back, hard single-source drama. ENVIRONMENT + ATMOSPHERE: Intimate-to-revealing — starts ECU private (the application moment is hers alone) then pulls back to include the viewer in the reveal. AUDIO: Music ducks to -24dB at 4.5s for VO impact (single synth note holds, drums pause), ambient (lipstick-on-lip application sound 0.0-2.0s, lip-press-pop at 2.5s, lipstick cap click at 7.0s), VO [AIRA, electric peak, 150 wpm deliberate]: "Theek hai." pause 0.6s "Now they'll know." — delivery: "Theek hai" (okay/fine) thrown casual but loaded (Hindi dismissal-of-doubt), deliberate pause where camera arrives at CU, "Now they'll know" with final certainty and slight volume drop (not louder = scarier), eyes locked on camera throughout. DURATION: 8 seconds. FRAME RATE: 24fps. MOTION BLUR: 180-degree shutter, pull-back creating depth shift, lipstick stroke with precision blur, lip-press smooth. LIP-SYNC: Hindi "Theek hai" then English — freshly painted red lip articulating precisely. TEMPORAL LOGIC: 0.0-2.0s lipstick stroke (ECU), 2.0-2.5s lip-press-pop, 2.5-4.0s camera pulls back revealing full face, 4.0-5.0s settle and brow-raise, 5.0-6.5s VO delivery, 6.5-7.0s lipstick set-down-click, 7.0-8.0s held direct stare.

NEGATIVE: morphing, warping, identity drift, limb teleport, object pop-in, frame skip, mirrored composition, text overlay, watermark, AI artifact, ghosting, double exposure unless intended, lip-sync drift, audio desync, wardrobe drift between shots, unmotivated camera shake, physics violation (water/fire/hair/fabric), mannequin posture, frozen background, identity flicker.

### Frame 5 — Video (Near Complete — Gown)

SHOT TYPE: WS to Cowboy. CAMERA MOVEMENT: Slow orbit counter-clockwise (quarter-turn from 3/4-front to full-frontal over 8 seconds, orbiting around Aira in gown to reveal the sculpted-shoulder architecture from multiple angles). LENS: 35mm. SUBJECT ACTION: Aira standing in full crimson gown, just put on — at 0.0s adjusting shoulder drape with right hand, at 2.0s smoothing hip with left hand, at 3.5s settling into final stance (hand on hip, chin up). Remains in power-pose as camera orbits for remaining seconds, making micro-adjustments — slight weight shift at 5.0s, hair-smoothing ponytail-check with one hand at 6.0s, then returns to stance. LIGHTING: Magenta key from left, orbit reveals how the crimson gown catches and releases light from changing angles, architectural shoulder creating complex shadow geometry. ENVIRONMENT + ATMOSPHERE: Full studio visible during orbit — mirror-wall, polished floor reflecting gown, haze catching light at different densities as camera moves through it, editorial scale and emptiness making her the absolute center. AUDIO: Music at -12dB (full beat at peak energy, synth melody driving, drums punching, 120 BPM — the music says "she's ready"), ambient (stiletto placement on concrete at 0.0s, fabric adjustment rustle, heel-click at 3.5s final stance), VO [AIRA, electric confident, 155 wpm]: "Crimson. Graphic liner. Ponytail like a weapon." beat "Not sorry." — delivery: Three items listed with staccato pace (each one a bullet point said fast), slight playfulness entering at "weapon" (the metaphor amuses her), "Not sorry" as afterthought that isn't — it's the manifesto. DURATION: 8 seconds. FRAME RATE: 24fps. MOTION BLUR: 180-degree shutter, orbit creating background-shift blur, gown fabric catching motion in orbit direction, smooth cinematic orbit. LIP-SYNC: English, staccato delivery with clear consonants, lips visible throughout orbit (front-facing across most of arc). TEMPORAL LOGIC: 0.0-2.0s shoulder adjust, 2.0-3.5s hip smooth and settle, 3.5-5.0s power-pose hold as orbit continues, 5.0-6.0s micro-adjustments, 6.0-8.0s final locked stance with VO completing.

NEGATIVE: morphing, warping, identity drift, limb teleport, object pop-in, frame skip, mirrored composition, text overlay, watermark, AI artifact, ghosting, double exposure unless intended, lip-sync drift, audio desync, wardrobe drift between shots, unmotivated camera shake, physics violation (water/fire/hair/fabric), mannequin posture, frozen background, identity flicker.

### Frame 6 — Video (The Reveal + Sign-off)

SHOT TYPE: Full Shot to MCU. CAMERA MOVEMENT: Dolly-in fast (aggressive push from Full Shot to MCU over 4 seconds — then STATIC lock for sign-off delivery in final 4 seconds, the camera aggressively approaching her like the world will). LENS: 35mm widening to 50mm equivalent through dolly distance. SUBJECT ACTION: Opening Full Shot — Aira in complete look, power stance, slight forward-lean toward camera (meeting its approach). As camera pushes in (0.0-4.0s), she holds position with growing intensity in expression — jaw setting, eyes narrowing, smile building. At 4.0s camera locks at MCU. At 4.5s delivers sign-off with single pointed finger at camera (index finger) then drops hand. At 6.5s slight wink (one-eyed, left). At 7.0s turns and begins walk toward studio exit (mirror-wall showing her retreating back). Final beat: her ponytail swaying as she walks away. LIGHTING: Magenta key at maximum intensity on face as camera arrives close (proximity to light source increasing with dolly-in), dramatic single-light on final expression, gown catching magenta richly. ENVIRONMENT + ATMOSPHERE: Studio editorial space, mirror-wall, the energy of departure — she is leaving (for the event), the studio was just preparation, now it's time. AUDIO: Music at -12dB (peak energy holding, full arrangement driving, 120 BPM), at 4.0s drums break for 0.5s (silence for sign-off setup), VO [AIRA, electric maximum, 130 wpm deliberate-slow-for-impact]: "Watch me." — delivery: Two words. Dropped low. Direct. Zero smile in voice (the face can smile, the voice is steel). The period is audible in the delivery. After sign-off: music hits back at full for exit walk. Ambient: stiletto clicks retreating, fabric whisper, door implied. DURATION: 8 seconds. FRAME RATE: 24fps. MOTION BLUR: 180-degree shutter, aggressive dolly-in creating strong depth shift, then locked still for sign-off, exit-walk with natural stride blur. LIP-SYNC: "Watch me" — minimal lip movement, deliberate, crisp W and M. TEMPORAL LOGIC: 0.0-4.0s dolly-in from Full to MCU (Aira holds stance meeting approach), 4.0-4.5s beat and VO setup, 4.5-5.0s "Watch me" delivery with pointed finger, 5.0-5.5s finger drops, 5.5-6.5s wink, 6.5-8.0s turn and exit-walk beginning.

NEGATIVE: morphing, warping, identity drift, limb teleport, object pop-in, frame skip, mirrored composition, text overlay, watermark, AI artifact, ghosting, double exposure unless intended, lip-sync drift, audio desync, wardrobe drift between shots, unmotivated camera shake, physics violation (water/fire/hair/fabric), mannequin posture, frozen background, identity flicker.


---

# CONCEPT 4 — GRWM

**Concept Line:** "The brunch is easy — the conversation waiting inside it is not."
**Format:** GRWM (Get Ready With Me)
**Stakes:** Getting ready for a Sunday morning brunch with the friend who ghosted me for three months
**Register:** CURIOUS-CONFIDENT
**Duration:** 40 seconds total
**Frames:** 5 frames x 8 seconds each
**Wardrobe Pillar:** Pillar 3 (Effortless Day) — cream linen wide-leg trouser + white cotton tank, minimal gold layered necklaces
**Hair:** HC-23 Air-Dried Boho — natural texture, loose soft waves, air-dried with scrunched volume, face-framing layers
**Makeup:** ML-5 Effortless Day — fresh dewy skin, peachy blush, tinted lip balm, soft brow, minimal mascara
**Setting:** GRWM Pillar 1 — Vanity / Dressing Table (white marble surface, soft morning window light, lived-in styling, products scattered naturally)
**Music:** Indie-acoustic soft-pop, 100 BPM, light guitar, subtle electronic undertone
**Opener:** "Three months. Zero texts."
**Sign-off:** "Achha, chalo... brunch it is."
**Voice Mode:** SPOKEN
**Signature Flag:** FULL
**Energy Arc:** Vulnerable (Frame 1) > Processing (Frame 2) > Decision (Frame 3) > Ready (Frame 4) > Loose (Frame 5)

## IMAGE PROMPTS

### Frame 1 — Opening State

ASPECT RATIO: 9:16 vertical. SUBJECT: AIRA — Adult woman late 20s-early 30s, South Asian (Indian), warm honey-to-caramel skin tone with golden undertone, 5'6"-5'8", soft-strong hourglass-athletic silhouette, fuller sculpted legs with toned thigh definition, fuller shapely thighs, fuller feminine arms with subtle muscle tone, fuller defined chest in proportion, flat toned midsection, defined waist clear waist-to-hip ratio, curvy hip line with natural feminine flare, heart-shaped to oval face, defined cheekbones, full defined lips with natural cupid's bow, almond-shaped expressive eyes dark brown iris with subtle amber flecks, strong but feminine groomed naturally arched brow, natural sun-kissed glow, long dark brown to near-black hair with subtle warm highlights naturally textured soft waves with body and movement, elegant well-groomed hands.

WARDROBE STATE (Frame 1): Oversized white linen button-down (boyfriend-shirt energy), unbuttoned at top three, hanging to mid-thigh over simple cotton shorts. Bare feet. Morning-undressed state.

HAIR STATE (Frame 1): Bedhead — slept-on-wet, one side slightly flattened, natural texture emerging, messy and authentic. No product, no styling.

MAKEUP STATE (Frame 1): Bare face. Morning skin — slightly puffy under-eyes from sleep, natural texture, bare lips slightly dry, brows natural and ungroomed. Fresh but undone.

HAND POSITIONS: Right hand holding coffee mug (ceramic, handmade-looking, half-full) at chest height mid-sip, fingers wrapped around mug body. Left hand resting on marble vanity surface, fingertips tapping once (nervous energy, the tap of someone processing).

FACIAL MICRO-DYNAMICS: Eyes — looking at phone propped on vanity (implied text conversation visible on screen), slight squint of processing/reading, left eye marginally more open, catchlight from window at 2 o'clock soft and warm, expression reading as bemused-skeptical. Brows — left raised singular in "really?" expression, right steady, natural ungroomed shape. Lips — pressed together in thought with coffee mug approaching, slight sideways purse (the face of "hmm"), pre-sip position. Cheeks — natural morning puffiness softening cheekbone edges, bare and warm. Jaw — slightly shifted right in thought-processing, relaxed. Breath — mid-exhale settling, morning casual.

BODY POSTURE: Standing at vanity, weight on left hip (casual morning lean), right hip cocked, spine in natural slight-S comfortable curve, left elbow on vanity for lean support. Barefoot morning ease.

KINETIC STILLNESS — Six Layers:
1. Subject micro-action: Left fingertips mid-tap on marble surface (nervous processing), mug approaching lips (mid-sip trajectory), slight weight-shift lean deepening
2. Fabric/hair state: Oversized shirt hanging with one side slightly higher from lean, collar fallen open, bedhead hair with one piece mid-fall across forehead from head-tilt, air-dry texture developing
3. Particulate layer: Morning dust motes in soft window light shaft, 12-15 particles drifting lazily in warm morning beam, coffee steam rising from mug in thin wisp catching light
4. Contact-point activity: Fingertips tapping marble (micro-vibration implied), mug warm in palm creating finger-wrap compression, bare feet on cool floor with toe-micro-curl
5. Background motion: Morning window with sheer curtain diffusing light (slight breeze micro-sway), phone screen on vanity with notification light pulsing, single fresh flower in small vase with petal micro-settling
6. Light in motion: Soft morning window light from camera-right (east, 6000K natural cool-warm), gentle and diffused through sheer, coffee steam catching light and dispersing, mug surface with warm liquid-shimmer

SPATIAL LOGIC:
- FOREGROUND: Vanity surface with scattered morning products (moisturizer, lip balm, hair clips), phone propped with screen visible, coffee ring stain on marble — lived-in and real. Slightly soft focus.
- MIDGROUND: Aira in morning lean, sharp focus, coffee and phone interaction as narrative setup
- BACKGROUND: Bedroom behind vanity — unmade bed edge visible, window with sheer curtain and morning light, small plant on windowsill. Soft warm focus.

LIGHTING: Key: Soft morning window from camera-right, diffused through sheer, 5800K natural. Fill: Room ambient at -2 stops warm bounce. Rim: Window edge-light on left shoulder thin and soft. Practical: Phone screen glow on face (subtle). Light separation: Subject 1.5 stops brighter than background.

FRAMING: MCU / Bust — top of head with 8% headroom to mid-chest. Subject 72% of frame. Camera height: eye level. Body angle: 3/4 casual lean. Lookroom: toward phone/vanity camera-left.

LENS: 50mm. APERTURE: f/2.2 — subject sharp, vanity foreground soft, background bedroom soft with warm morning bokeh.

ATMOSPHERE: Sunday morning ease, lived-in warmth, natural light, the quiet processing of someone who just received an unexpected text. Coffee steam and dust motes as life-confirmation. Kodak Portra 400 morning warmth.

COLOR GRADE: Soft warm morning — cream/white dominant (shirt, marble, walls), warm skin tones natural, coffee brown as accent, soft greens from plant, overall light and airy with slight warmth lift. Lifted blacks (morning brightness), gentle contrast.

MAKEUP STATE (Frame 5 — COMPLETE): ML-5 Effortless Day achieved. Dewy fresh skin. Soft brows. Light mascara. Peachy blush. Tinted lip balm. The complete "no-makeup makeup" look that reads effortlessly beautiful.

HAND POSITIONS: Right hand reaching for door handle (apartment door, heading out), fingers wrapping around handle mid-grasp. Left hand holding phone at hip (checking time or last message), screen angled toward camera so glow visible on face.

FACIAL MICRO-DYNAMICS: Eyes — slight side-glance back toward camera (the over-shoulder-glance-back exit beat), relaxed and warm with slight amusement, the "wish me luck" expression, left eye visible in the 3/4 angle, catchlight from phone and door-hallway light. Brows — raised slightly (the "here goes nothing" expression), easy and open. Lips — closed full smile, genuine warmth, the Duchenne smile (eyes crinkle first, cheeks lift, then lips spread), lip balm sheen catching light, the face of someone who has accepted what is coming. Cheeks — smile-lifted, blush visible and glowing, natural crinkle at outer eye from genuine smile. Jaw — relaxed and open, easy, the looseness of resolved energy. Breath — post-exhale easy, the breath of departure, leaving.

BODY POSTURE: Standing at door, slight turn back toward camera (3/4 rear angle with face turned over right shoulder), weight shifting forward into departure-stride, right arm extended to door, left relaxed at side with phone. Dynamic exit-energy posture.

KINETIC STILLNESS — Six Layers:
1. Subject micro-action: Right hand mid-grasp of door handle, slight turn-back-over-shoulder caught at full expression, weight transferring forward for exit stride
2. Fabric/hair state: Linen trousers with walking-motion drape beginning, bag strap settling on shoulder, air-dried hair swinging from over-shoulder turn with one face-framing piece flying, sunglasses on head slightly askew from turn
3. Particulate layer: Hallway light dust motes visible through cracked door, 6-8 particles in bright doorway light, morning freshness implied
4. Contact-point activity: Fingers wrapping door handle creating metal-contact, phone in left hand with thumb-on-screen pressure, sandal ball-of-foot pressing into floor for departure push
5. Background motion: Door opening revealing bright hallway beyond (the world), apartment behind her organized and morning-complete, single leaf on plant shifting from door-breeze
6. Light in motion: Bright hallway light flooding in through opening door creating strong backlight/rim on figure, morning window still present but door-light now competing, creating dual-source dynamic

SPATIAL LOGIC: FG: Door frame and handle in immediate foreground, slightly soft, Aira's reaching hand connecting to it. MG: Aira at door in 3/4 rear with face turned back, sharp focus, the exit moment. BG: Apartment interior behind her (vanity area, bed, morning-complete space), soft focus, warm.

LIGHTING: Key: Hallway light from door-opening camera-left at 5500K, strong and bright creating rim and fill on turned face. Fill: Morning window from interior. Rim: Hallway light wrapping fully around figure from front. Light separation: 2 stops brighter doorway creating exit-light drawing.

FRAMING: MS / Waist — top of head 8% headroom to mid-thigh. Subject 55% of frame. Camera height: eye level. Body angle: 3/4 rear with face turned over shoulder toward camera. Lookroom: toward camera-right where her gaze returns.

LENS: 35mm. f/2.8. Full scene depth — subject sharp, door frame foreground soft, apartment background soft.

COMPOSITION REFERENCE: The over-shoulder farewell — Spielberg emotional staging for departures. Leading line of door frame drawing eye to subject. Light drawing subject toward exit.

ATMOSPHERE: Sunday morning departure, easy and resolved, the lightness of going to meet something uncertain with confidence and humor, bright and fresh and forward-moving. The loop point — her look-back is the re-watch trigger. Portra 400 brightness.

COLOR GRADE: Bright and fresh — cream, white, warm skin, bright hallway light blowing slightly, lifted everywhere, minimal shadow, the airy optimism of someone choosing to show up. Clean and effortless.

NEGATIVE: mirrored, flipped, inverted, extra limbs, fused fingers, melted features, asymmetric eyes (unintentional), garbled text, floating shadows, duplicated subjects, low-res patches, plastic skin, oversharpened, AI-generated artifacts, watermarks, signature, deformed hands, malformed teeth, joint cuts at ankle/knee/wrist/elbow/neck, amputated fingertips, cross-eyed, lazy eye, off-axis pupils, melted clothing, shoes-not-touching-ground, mismatched footwear pair, mannequin-stiff posture, dead eyes, statue-frozen energy.

## VIDEO PROMPTS

### Frame 1 — Video

SHOT TYPE: MCU. CAMERA MOVEMENT: Static with micro-handheld drift (intimate proximity, barely perceptible breathing movement). LENS: 50mm. SUBJECT ACTION: Aira at vanity in morning shirt, coffee in hand, reading phone. At 0.5s slight eyebrow raise at phone screen. At 1.0s looks up to camera, slight head-shake. At 1.2s VO begins while she sips coffee at 3.0s. Sets mug down at 4.5s. Slight left-hand tap on vanity surface (processing). LIGHTING: Soft morning window right, diffused sheer, warm ambient. ENVIRONMENT: Vanity morning setting, coffee, phone, products scattered, lived-in bedroom. AUDIO: Music at -24dB (acoustic guitar gentle intro, 100 BPM barely present), ambient (coffee sip, mug-on-marble set-down, phone notification chime at 0.0s), VO [AIRA, curious-confident, 150 wpm light pace]: "Three months. Zero texts." breath "And now she wants brunch?" slight laugh "Achha." — delivery: "Three months" flat declarative, "Zero texts" same flat (building absurdity through flatness), breath, "And now she wants brunch?" with rising incredulous-amused inflection, light scoff-laugh, "Achha" (Hindi okay/really) as single loaded word with head-tilt. DURATION: 8s. FRAME RATE: 24fps. MOTION BLUR: 180-degree. LIP-SYNC: English with Hindi "Achha" — conversational, natural.

NEGATIVE: morphing, warping, identity drift, limb teleport, object pop-in, frame skip, mirrored composition, text overlay, watermark, AI artifact, ghosting, double exposure unless intended, lip-sync drift, audio desync, wardrobe drift between shots, unmotivated camera shake, physics violation (water/fire/hair/fabric), mannequin posture, frozen background, identity flicker.

---

# CONCEPT 5 — GRWM

**Concept Line:** "The cover they never thought I'd get — and the woman in the mirror who always knew."
**Format:** GRWM (Get Ready With Me)
**Stakes:** Getting ready for the photoshoot that could change everything — first solo cover
**Register:** TENDER
**Duration:** 48 seconds total
**Frames:** 6 frames x 8 seconds each
**Wardrobe Pillar:** Pillar 11 (Sensual Editorial Celebrity) — black bias-cut silk satin slip dress floor-length with thin spaghetti straps, liquid drape following every curve
**Hair:** HC-8 Deep-Side-Part Cascade — dramatic deep side part on left, hair cascading over right shoulder in voluminous glossy waves, left side pinned behind ear
**Makeup:** ML-16 Glossy-Lip Hero — luminous skin, soft bronze eye, strong defined brow, glossy nude-pink lip as hero feature
**Setting:** GRWM Pillar 3 — Bedroom Golden Hour (full-length mirror, bed-edge seating, golden afternoon shaft, warm haze, wardrobe visible)
**Music:** R&B-slow minimalist beat, 80 BPM, bass-heavy, intimate, sparse
**Opener:** "Yeh moment... I've been waiting."
**Sign-off:** "Bas. Ready."
**Voice Mode:** SPOKEN
**Signature Flag:** FULL
**Energy Arc:** Vulnerable (Frame 1) > Processing (Frames 2-3) > Decision/Tenderness (Frame 4) > Ready (Frame 5) > Loose/Powerful (Frame 6)

## IMAGE PROMPTS

### Frame 1 — Opening State

ASPECT RATIO: 9:16 vertical. SUBJECT: AIRA — Adult woman late 20s-early 30s, South Asian (Indian), warm honey-to-caramel skin tone with golden undertone, 5'6"-5'8", soft-strong hourglass-athletic silhouette, fuller sculpted legs with toned thigh definition, fuller shapely thighs, fuller feminine arms with subtle muscle tone, fuller defined chest in proportion, flat toned midsection, defined waist clear waist-to-hip ratio, curvy hip line with natural feminine flare, heart-shaped to oval face, defined cheekbones, full defined lips with natural cupid's bow, almond-shaped expressive eyes dark brown iris with subtle amber flecks, strong but feminine groomed naturally arched brow, natural sun-kissed glow, long dark brown to near-black hair with subtle warm highlights naturally textured soft waves with body and movement, elegant well-groomed hands.

WARDROBE STATE (Frame 1): Nude silk slip (short, mid-thigh), bare legs crossed at ankle, hair robe draped on shoulders open at front. Intimate pre-shoot state.

HAIR STATE (Frame 1): Freshly blow-dried (smooth, voluminous, not yet styled into deep side-part), hanging naturally with body and movement, slight wave from blowout.

MAKEUP STATE (Frame 1): Bare face with fresh skincare glow — skin prepped and hydrated (serum sheen visible), no foundation yet. Clean canvas pre-glam.

HAND POSITIONS: Right hand touching collarbone (self-soothing tender gesture), fingers resting lightly on sternum. Left hand holding a single printed page (the call sheet for the shoot) resting on left thigh, text blurred but presence meaningful.

FACIAL MICRO-DYNAMICS: Eyes — soft and contemplative gazing at own reflection in full-length mirror, slight widening suggesting the enormity of the moment registering, moisture at inner corners (pride, disbelief, tenderness), dark brown with amber flecks catching golden afternoon light, catchlight at 2 o'clock warm and round. Brows — slightly raised together (vulnerable wonder), inner-brow pull upward creating soft questioning expression. Lips — parted on breath, the breath before words form, soft and bare, natural pink-brown, lower lip fuller from relaxed state. Cheeks — bare and dewy from skincare, natural warmth, soft and touchable without product. Jaw — soft, slightly dropped in the openness of emotion, throat pulse visible. Breath — deep slow inhale, the gathering breath before speaking something significant, shoulders rising slowly.

BODY POSTURE: Seated at bed edge, legs crossed at ankle, spine with slight forward curve (intimate, not posed), weight shifted right creating natural asymmetry, head tilted slightly right (tender vulnerability). The posture of someone having a private moment with themselves before the world arrives.

KINETIC STILLNESS — Six Layers:
1. Subject micro-action: Right hand fingertips mid-settle on collarbone (just placed, settling into contact), inhale lifting chest under fingertips, the self-holding gesture of tenderness
2. Fabric/hair state: Silk slip catching golden hour beam creating liquid highlights along bias-cut drape, hair with post-blowout body catching light in soft movement from head-tilt, robe lapel beginning to slip off left shoulder
3. Particulate layer: Golden hour dust motes filling bedroom air (15-20 particles visible), afternoon light creating volumetric golden beam from window crossing at 45 degrees, warm and slow-drifting
4. Contact-point activity: Fingertips on collarbone creating skin-warmth connection, call sheet paper resting on thigh with weight-crinkle, seated on bed creating mattress-compression visible at hip
5. Background motion: Golden light shaft moving imperceptibly across room as afternoon sun descends, sheer curtain with gentle billow inward from slightly open window, garment bag (containing the black slip dress for shoot) hanging on closet door with slight sway
6. Light in motion: Golden hour beam (4:00 PM quality) crossing room diagonally, catching airborne particles, creating warm gradient across wall, rim-wrapping around right side of hair creating golden halo edge, light intensifying/softening with outdoor cloud passage

SPATIAL LOGIC: FG: Bed surface with call sheet slightly out of focus, providing narrative context. MG: Aira seated, sharp focus, tender opening moment. BG: Bedroom — full-length mirror reflecting her, garment bag with shoot dress visible, window with golden light, warm afternoon atmosphere. Soft golden bokeh.

LIGHTING: Key: Golden hour window from camera-left, 3200K warm, medium-hard beam. Fill: Room ambient at -2 stops from wall bounce, warm. Rim: Golden wrap on right side of hair and shoulder. Practical: None. Light separation: 1.5 stops.

FRAMING: MCU/Bust — top of head 8% headroom to mid-chest. Subject 74%. Eye level. 3/4 turn. Lookroom toward mirror camera-right.

LENS: 50mm. f/2.0. Subject sharp, foreground bed surface soft, background golden and soft.

COMPOSITION REFERENCE: Bradford Young intimate skin-priority, golden ratio placement, warm underexposed emotional approach.

ATMOSPHERE: Tender afternoon golden hour, the intimate privacy before professional transformation, golden particles suggesting magic in the ordinary, the weight of a dream about to become real. Kodak 5207 warmth, grain.

# CONCEPT 6 — BEAUTY AD (Cinematic Beauty Hero)

**Concept Line:** "Liquid gold settling into skin like a memory of warmth."
**Format:** Cinematic Beauty Hero Ad
**Product:** Luxury serum — frosted glass column bottle, brushed gold pipette cap, honey-amber liquid with visible viscosity, embossed monogram on glass, weighted base, light refracts through formula creating amber caustics
**Mood Archetype:** MA-2 "honey on skin"
**Sub-type:** Cinematic Beauty Hero
**Duration:** 12 seconds total
**Frames:** 4 frames x 3 seconds each
**Register:** REVERENT
**Voice:** SILENT
**Product Performance Move:** P-1 Slow Levitation Hover (product lifts from surface and hovers at collarbone height with shadow beneath, restrained luxury)
**Camera:** Orbital quarter-turn on hero product (slow CW orbit, revealing product dimensionally)
**Setting:** B-3 Golden-Hour Bedroom (vanity surface, golden shaft from west window, dust motes, warm haze, marble surface)
**Wardrobe:** Cream silk slip, bare shoulders, minimal
**Hair:** HC-7 Center-Part Column — sleek center-parted hair falling straight as columns on either side of face, glossy and controlled
**Makeup:** ML-3 Clean Editorial — perfected matte skin, groomed brow, nude lip, no color distraction from product
**Color Grade:** Warm Kodak Portra 400, golden highlights, lifted blacks, honey midtones
**Object Design Block:** Frosted glass column bottle 12cm height, 3cm diameter cylinder with subtle taper toward cap. Brushed gold pipette cap with fine knurling for grip. Honey-amber liquid formula visible through frosted glass as warm glow. Embossed monogram on glass surface catching raking light. Weighted glass base with polished flat bottom creating contact shadow. When light passes through, amber caustic patterns project onto nearby surfaces. Pipette dropper visible inside cap as gold metal rod with black rubber bulb.

## IMAGE PROMPTS

### Frame 1 — Product Hero (Levitation Begin)

ASPECT RATIO: 9:16 vertical. SUBJECT: AIRA — Adult woman late 20s-early 30s, South Asian (Indian), warm honey-to-caramel skin tone with golden undertone, 5'6"-5'8", soft-strong hourglass-athletic silhouette, fuller sculpted legs with toned thigh definition, fuller shapely thighs, fuller feminine arms with subtle muscle tone, fuller defined chest in proportion, flat toned midsection, defined waist clear waist-to-hip ratio, curvy hip line with natural feminine flare, heart-shaped to oval face, defined cheekbones, full defined lips with natural cupid's bow, almond-shaped expressive eyes dark brown iris with subtle amber flecks, strong but feminine groomed naturally arched brow, natural sun-kissed glow, long dark brown to near-black hair with subtle warm highlights naturally textured soft waves with body and movement, elegant well-groomed hands.

WARDROBE STATE: Cream silk slip, thin straps on shoulders, bare collarbones visible. Minimal and retreated to let product be hero.

HAIR STATE: HC-7 Center-Part Column — sleek center-parted, straight glossy curtains of hair framing face, falling past shoulders.

MAKEUP STATE: ML-3 Clean Editorial complete — perfected base, matte, groomed brow, nude lip, no distracting color.

PRODUCT STATE: Serum bottle mid-levitation — hovering 5cm above marble vanity surface, shadow beneath visible on marble (confirming it's hovering, not suspended from above), bottle JUST lifting off surface (the birth of the levitation). Gold pipette cap catching golden hour light. Amber liquid inside with visible viscosity — settling lower as bottle rises (physics of liquid inside moving container). Frosted glass diffusing golden light passing through creating warm glow-aura around bottle.

HAND POSITIONS: Right hand at collarbone height, fingertips 3cm below the hovering bottle, palm up in gentle receiving-cup position (about to catch, or the gesture that encouraged the rise). Left hand at side relaxed, resting on vanity edge.

FACIAL MICRO-DYNAMICS: Eyes — gazing at the levitating product with soft reverent attention, slightly lowered lids (worship-gaze), catchlight warm from golden hour, pupils relaxed. Brows — settled and soft, no tension, pure contemplation. Lips — closed softly, neutral-to-slight upturn at corners, bare nude lip catching minimal light. Breath — slow exhale, reverent stillness.

BODY POSTURE: Standing at vanity, slight lean toward product (drawn to it), weight left, spine elongated, shoulders bare and open.

KINETIC STILLNESS — Six Layers:
1. Subject micro-action: Right palm fingers micro-spreading in receiving gesture, slight upward energy in fingertips encouraging the rise
2. Fabric/hair state: Cream slip catching golden shaft with liquid satin-highlight along bias-cut, hair curtains absolutely still (no breeze in this sacred moment), one strand of hair catching light creating bright line
3. Particulate layer: Golden dust motes suspended around the hovering bottle (20+ particles), some appearing to orbit it slowly, golden afternoon light making each mote luminous, creating halo of floating gold around the product
4. Contact-point activity: Bottle shadow on marble surface visible and defined (proving levitation height), shadow edge slightly diffused, right palm with fingertip-tension suggesting energy connection to product
5. Background motion: Bedroom beyond in golden warm haze, dust motes in background drifting slowly left-to-right, curtain absolutely still (sacred space), amber caustic light-patterns from product projected onto nearby marble surface
6. Light in motion: Golden hour shaft passing through frosted bottle creating amber caustics on marble below (moving slowly as sun descends), the light THROUGH the product creating its own moving-light performance

SPATIAL LOGIC: FG: Marble vanity surface with product shadow and amber caustics in lower 20%, slightly soft at edges. MG: Hovering bottle as primary hero + Aira's receiving hand, both sharp (dual-focus plane). BG: Aira's face and upper body as context (soft but recognizable), golden bedroom behind with afternoon light.

LIGHTING: Key: Golden hour shaft from camera-left at 35 degrees catching bottle directly (hard beam, 3000K, creating product-glow and caustics). Fill: Marble surface bounce providing under-fill on bottle at -2.5 stops. Rim: Golden wrap around Aira's bare right shoulder from window-angle. Practical: Product itself acts as practical light-modifier (amber liquid filtering and projecting light). Light separation: Product 2+ stops brighter than Aira (product is HERO, she is context). 1.5 stops subject above background.

FRAMING: MS — top of Aira's head with 10% headroom to vanity surface at bottom. Subject (Aira) 50% of frame but PRODUCT is hero at center-right. Product at rule-of-thirds right intersection. Beauty compositional priority on the levitation moment.

LENS: 85mm. APERTURE: f/2.0 — dual focus plane: product sharp AND nearby hand sharp, Aira's face at slightly softer plane (hero priority on product), background completely dissolved.

COMPOSITION REFERENCE: Slow Levitation + Orbital (gold-standard luxury hero pairing per Appendix 8). Product centered in light-path, Aira framing it with body and hand.

ATMOSPHERE: Sacred luxury, golden light treating the product as precious object, the reverence of beauty ritual, the impossible moment of levitation rendered with physical conviction (shadow, light, viscosity all behaving correctly). Kodak Portra 400.

COLOR GRADE: Warm golden — honey-amber from product formula dominating the color story, golden-hour warmth, marble cool-neutral as base, Aira's skin warm-honey, cream slip retreating. Lifted blacks, golden highlights, rich amber midtones. Portra 400 warmth.

NEGATIVE: mirrored, flipped, inverted, extra limbs, fused fingers, melted features, asymmetric eyes (unintentional), garbled text, floating shadows, duplicated subjects, low-res patches, plastic skin, oversharpened, AI-generated artifacts, watermarks, signature, deformed hands, malformed teeth, joint cuts at ankle/knee/wrist/elbow/neck, amputated fingertips, cross-eyed, lazy eye, off-axis pupils, melted clothing, shoes-not-touching-ground, mismatched footwear pair, mannequin-stiff posture, dead eyes, statue-frozen energy.

### Frame 3 — Pipette Drop (Product in Use)

ASPECT RATIO: 9:16 vertical. # CONCEPT 7 — BEAUTY AD (Fragrance Mood Piece)

**Concept Line:** "A scent that arrives before you do and stays after you leave."
**Format:** Fragrance Mood Piece
**Product:** Perfume — hand-blown asymmetric bulb bottle in artisan irregular shape, oxidized bronze stopper with aged patina, smoked amber glass (semi-transparent with visible imperfections), no label only sculptural form (shape IS brand), weighted heavy base, organic irregular silhouette, warm amber-gold formula visible through glass with slight cloudiness suggesting botanical infusion
**Mood Archetype:** MA-20 "fragrance unfolding on bare collarbone"
**Sub-type:** Fragrance Mood Piece
**Duration:** 24 seconds total
**Frames:** 5 frames x ~5 seconds each (4.8s per frame)
**Register:** CONTEMPLATIVE
**Voice:** SILENT (single whispered word "...sach" at peak frame 4)
**Product Performance Move:** P-16 Smoke/Mist Birth (fragrance mist materializes from nothing around product, suggesting scent made visible)
**Camera:** Slow push-in from MS to ECU across reel (progressive intimacy)
**Setting:** B-3 Golden-Hour Bedroom (sheer curtain, golden particles, warm haze, intimate late-afternoon)
**Wardrobe:** Ivory silk robe falling off one shoulder, bare skin as canvas for fragrance
**Hair:** HC-4 Soft Hollywood waves — side-swept, voluminous, warm-highlighted
**Makeup:** ML-7 Skin-First — luminous bare skin with minimal intervention, hydrated and dewy
**Color Grade:** Warm amber midtones, lifted shadows, subtle halation on highlights
**Object Design Block:** Hand-blown asymmetric bulb bottle — no two sides identical, organic flowing form 9cm height, widest point 6cm. Smoked amber glass semi-transparent (formula visible inside as darker amber shadow). Oxidized bronze stopper with natural patina (irregular texture, not polished). No label, no text, purely sculptural. Weighted base with pontil mark from hand-blowing visible at bottom. When backlit, glass glows with internal amber warmth. Surface has subtle hand-blown irregularities (stretch marks in glass, micro-bubbles frozen mid-glass).

# CONCEPT 8 — BEAUTY AD (Product Launch)

**Concept Line:** "One click. One swipe. The room already knows."
**Format:** Product Launch Ad
**Product:** Matte lipstick — magnetic-snap heavy bullet, full brushed rose-gold metal body with satin finish, satisfying mechanical click on open/close, embossed brand mark on cap in debossed serif, deep crimson formula with velvet-matte finish, tapered ergonomic barrel, weighted substantial feel, minimal design with no visible label (form IS identity), bullet emerges with precise click-stop mechanism
**Mood Archetype:** MA-22 "lips parting before words"
**Sub-type:** Product Launch Ad
**Duration:** 24 seconds total
**Frames:** 6 frames x 4 seconds each
**Register:** ELECTRIC
**Voice:** SELECTIVE — single tagline "One swipe. Done."
**Product Performance Move:** P-9 Self-Opening Cap (cap magnetically releases and lifts independently, revealing bullet)
**Camera:** Macro push-in on lips + vertical tilt reveal
**Setting:** B-1 Mirror-Wall Studio (polished concrete floor, single hard magenta key, clean haze, minimal)
**Wardrobe:** Black minimalist silk shell + tailored black trouser (retreating wardrobe, letting product be color-hero)
**Hair:** HC-9 Slicked-Back Wet — full gel-slick from forehead to nape, tight and sharp, no loose strands
**Makeup:** ML-11 Bold Lip Statement (building across reel — bare lip transforming to full crimson payoff)
**Color Grade:** High contrast, magenta-tinted rim, crushed shadows, chrome highlights
**Object Design Block:** Magnetic-snap heavy bullet lipstick — full brushed rose-gold metal body 8.5cm height, weighty in hand (30g+), satisfying magnetic closure that clicks audibly. Cap with embossed brand monogram (debossed into metal). Bullet mechanism smooth twist-up with no play/wobble. Formula visible: deep crimson velvet-matte, bullet shape precision-molded with clean point. Metal body catches light as brushed specular (directional grain in metal visible). When opened, internal mechanism visible as precision engineering (threaded brass interior). The cap removal reveals the crimson with maximum color-contrast against rose-gold.

## IMAGE PROMPTS

### Frame 1 — Product Hero (Self-Opening Cap)

ASPECT RATIO: 9:16 vertical. 5. Background motion: Mirror-wall reflecting the self-opening moment from behind, studio haze drift left-to-right in magenta beam
6. Light in motion: Magenta key catching rose-gold body creating warm-pink specular along metal grain, cap hovering creating moving shadow below as it lifts, crimson formula catching magenta and reading vivid red-pink

FRAMING: Product-priority — lipstick at center-frame occupying 20% of frame as sharp hero, Aira behind as context at 50% subject. Camera height slightly below product (looking up at the opening moment).

Product metal against skin (temperature contrast implied) 5. Mirror-wall showing full figure from behind 6. Magenta key at peak on product + lip creating color rhyme

LIGHTING: Magenta key on both product (rose-gold) and lip (crimson) simultaneously — the product and its result in the same light creating visual equation.

FRAMING: Beauty Crop — head to collarbone. 80% subject. Product beside face. The beauty-hero-shot.

### Frame 6 — Lip Part (Final)

ASPECT RATIO: 9:16 vertical. SUBJECT: AIRA — Adult woman late 20s-early 30s, South Asian (Indian), warm honey-to-caramel skin tone with golden undertone, 5'6"-5'8", soft-strong hourglass-athletic silhouette, fuller sculpted legs with toned thigh definition, fuller shapely thighs, fuller feminine arms with subtle muscle tone, fuller defined chest in proportion, flat toned midsection, defined waist clear waist-to-hip ratio, curvy hip line with natural feminine flare, heart-shaped to oval face, defined cheekbones, full defined lips with natural cupid's bow, almond-shaped expressive eyes dark brown iris with subtle amber flecks, strong but feminine groomed naturally arched brow, natural sun-kissed glow, long dark brown to near-black hair with subtle warm highlights naturally textured soft waves with body and movement, elegant well-groomed hands. WARDROBE/HAIR: Unchanged. MAKEUP: Complete.

PRODUCT STATE: Set aside (on surface in background, hero role complete). Now the RESULT is the only hero — the lip on Aira performing in the world.

HAND POSITIONS: Both at sides, relaxed. Body standing powerful. Product no longer needed in hand — it has done its job.

FACIAL MICRO-DYNAMICS: Eyes — direct to camera, half-lidded and powerful, electric satisfaction. Lips — crimson matte, NOW slightly parted (MA-22 "lips parting before words") — the 2mm part between upper and lower lip creating the moment-before-speech that is the most sensual lip-state, crimson visible on inner lip surfaces, the parting suggesting she is about to speak. The final frame per mood archetype. Breath — about to speak (never does — the reel ends on potential).

KINETIC STILLNESS: 1. Lip-part caught at perfect 2mm separation (the held potential of words-about-to-come) 2. Chrome hair still 3. Sparse particles 4. The parted-lip as micro-action (muscles holding the open) 5. Lipstick on surface in BG (completed journey from product to result) 6. Magenta light between parted lips creating a thin bright line (the light enters the gap)

LIGHTING: Magenta on parted lips — the key finding the gap between lips and creating a thin bright line there. Maximum drama on the lip-part.

FRAMING: Choker — chin to forehead. 92% subject. The tightest possible frame for maximum lip impact.

LENS: 85mm. f/1.8.

COMPOSITION REFERENCE: High-contrast editorial beauty (Fincher precision, Kubrick symmetry), product-performance-as-hero framing.

# CONCEPT 9 — BEAUTY AD (Sensory Beauty Tutorial)

**Concept Line:** "The skin remembers warmth long after the morning leaves."
**Format:** Sensory Beauty Tutorial
**Product:** Cream blush compact — faceted glass body with brushed brass screw-top lid, multi-sided glass catching and refracting light at different angles, warm peach formula inside (creamy, buildable), mirror inside lid, weighted and satisfying to hold
**Mood Archetype:** MA-19 "skin remembering the day"
**Sub-type:** Sensory Beauty Tutorial
**Duration:** 20 seconds total
**Frames:** 5 frames x 4 seconds each
**Register:** KNOWING
**Voice:** SPOKEN — intimate instructional "Fingertip. Tap twice. Blend up... bas, that's it."
**Product Performance Move:** P-22 Wind-Animated Stillness (product stable on surface while hair and fabric move around it from gentle breeze — product as calm center)
**Camera:** Beauty ECU push-in on cheek application
**Setting:** B-4 Dawn Balcony (cool morning light from east-facing window/door, city skyline BG soft and distant, slight morning haze, fresh air energy)
**Wardrobe:** Cream cashmere mock-neck, soft and touchable, retreating wardrobe for skin-focus
**Hair:** HC-25 Morning Coffee Wave — effortless, slept-in texture, natural soft wave with volume, unbrushed beauty
**Makeup:** ML-2 Soft Nude (building — adding blush as tutorial subject, skin dewy with minimal base)
**Color Grade:** Soft natural daylight, warm-shift on skin priority, Portra grain
**Object Design Block:** Faceted glass compact body — hexagonal cross-section creating 6 flat faces each catching light at different angles. Brushed brass screw-top lid with fine knurling for grip and satisfying twist-open action. Glass body 6cm diameter, 2.5cm height. Warm peach cream formula inside (visible when opened) with smooth untouched surface showing brand deboss. Mirror inset inside lid (oval, slightly convex). Total weight 85g+ (satisfying heft). When light hits faceted glass, each face creates different refraction/reflection creating sparkle-array.

## IMAGE PROMPTS

### Frame 1 — Opening (Product in Light + Wind)

ASPECT RATIO: 9:16 vertical. SUBJECT: AIRA — Adult woman late 20s-early 30s, South Asian (Indian), warm honey-to-caramel skin tone with golden undertone, 5'6"-5'8", soft-strong hourglass-athletic silhouette, fuller sculpted legs with toned thigh definition, fuller shapely thighs, fuller feminine arms with subtle muscle tone, fuller defined chest in proportion, flat toned midsection, defined waist clear waist-to-hip ratio, curvy hip line with natural feminine flare, heart-shaped to oval face, defined cheekbones, full defined lips with natural cupid's bow, almond-shaped expressive eyes dark brown iris with subtle amber flecks, strong but feminine groomed naturally arched brow, natural sun-kissed glow, long dark brown to near-black hair with subtle warm highlights naturally textured soft waves with body and movement, elegant well-groomed hands.

4. Contact-point activity: Coffee mug warmth in left hand (steam rising implying temperature), fingertips about to contact glass (anticipation), product on stone ledge with weight-stable contact (grounded, unmoved by wind)
5. Background motion: City skyline soft and distant in morning haze, morning light changing (dawn progressing), distant movement (city waking), curtain/door fabric behind billowing from breeze
6. Light in motion: Cool dawn light (6000K blue-white) from east on faces of compact creating sparkle, light warming by the second as dawn progresses, glass facets each refracting different dawn-color based on angle

SPATIAL LOGIC: FG: Compact on stone ledge in lower-right frame area, faceted glass catching dawn light from multiple angles, sharp (product as hero even in establishing shot). MG: Aira reaching for it, sharp, morning state. BG: Dawn sky with city skyline silhouette, soft haze, pale blue-pink dawn colors.

LIGHTING: Key: Dawn light from camera-right (east), cool 6000K natural, medium-soft (pre-direct-sun). Fill: Sky ambient from above at -1.5 stops, cool blue. Rim: Dawn edge-light on left side of face from reflected sky. Practical: None. Light separation: Subject and product 1.5 stops above background sky.

FRAMING: MS — head to hip. Subject 55%. Eye level. Product on ledge at lower frame. Both subject and product visible in environmental context.

LENS: 50mm. f/2.2. Both subject and product in acceptable focus, background city soft with dawn-haze.

COMPOSITION REFERENCE: Rule of thirds — product at lower-right intersection, Aira's face at upper-left. Lubezki natural-light dawn approach.

ATMOSPHERE: Fresh dawn morning, outdoor air and breeze, the ritual of morning beauty in natural light, wind as character (animating everything except the grounded product), morning freshness and beginning energy. Portra 400 dawn grain.

### Frame 4 — Blend (Upward Stroke)

ASPECT RATIO: 9:16 vertical. SUBJECT: AIRA — Adult woman late 20s-early 30s, South Asian (Indian), warm honey-to-caramel skin tone with golden undertone, 5'6"-5'8", soft-strong hourglass-athletic silhouette, fuller sculpted legs with toned thigh definition, fuller shapely thighs, fuller feminine arms with subtle muscle tone, fuller defined chest in proportion, flat toned midsection, defined waist clear waist-to-hip ratio, curvy hip line with natural feminine flare, heart-shaped to oval face, defined cheekbones, full defined lips with natural cupid's bow, almond-shaped expressive eyes dark brown iris with subtle amber flecks, strong but feminine groomed naturally arched brow, natural sun-kissed glow, long dark brown to near-black hair with subtle warm highlights naturally textured soft waves with body and movement, elegant well-groomed hands.

Blush now visible on BOTH cheeks (left completed off-camera, right being blended NOW). The warm peach flush spreading and diffusing into skin seamlessly.

# CONCEPT 10 — BEAUTY AD (Beauty Editorial Film)

**Concept Line:** "Almost gold — the light between polish and something wilder."
**Format:** Beauty Editorial Film
**Product:** Highlighter — sculptural clamshell compact, hammered brass finish exterior with organic curved form (no straight lines), weighted satisfyingly in palm, golden-champagne powder formula inside with micro-shimmer particles visible, soft-focus finish on skin, interior mirror with brass frame, magnetic closure with subtle snap, each surface facet catching light differently, artisan metalwork aesthetic
**Mood Archetype:** MA-17 "the gleam beneath polished surfaces"
**Sub-type:** Beauty Editorial Film
**Duration:** 32 seconds total
**Frames:** 6 frames x ~5 seconds each (5.3s per frame)
**Register:** REVERENT
**Voice:** SILENT (poetry fragment VO "...almost gold" at frame 4)
**Product Performance Move:** P-14 Bloom Reveal (compact opens like mechanical flower — clamshell halves separating and rotating outward in organic unfolding motion)
**Camera:** Slow orbit quarter-turn + vertical tilt (combined across the reel — orbit in frames 1-3, vertical tilt in frames 4-6)
**Setting:** B-7 Minimalist Gallery (white plaster walls, single skylight overhead, negative space dominant, clean architectural space, polished pale-wood floor)
**Wardrobe:** Pillar 9 sculptural angular dress, monochrome silver — structured architectural mini dress with sharp geometric shoulders, liquid silver fabric
**Hair:** HC-26 Sculptural Architectural Bun — severe high bun pulled tight, structured and geometric, showing full face/neck architecture
**Makeup:** ML-26 Chrome-Lid — silver-chrome metallic eyeshadow on lids, strong sculpted brow, bare-nude lip, highlighted skin with champagne sheen (building with product)
**Color Grade:** High-key whites, controlled rolloff, minimal saturation, chrome accents only
**Object Design Block:** Sculptural clamshell compact — organic curved form with NO straight lines or hard angles, 7cm at widest, 5cm depth when closed. Hammered brass exterior with hand-finished irregular texture (each hammer mark visible at macro, warm metallic). Opens as clamshell (two halves connected by living hinge at back). Inside: golden-champagne powder formula with micro-shimmer particles visible in raking light (catches light as hundreds of tiny points). Interior pan is shallow curved bowl shape. Magnetic closure (satisfying click when closed). When closed: sculptural art object. When opened: functional beauty tool. Weight: 95g+ (satisfying, precious). P-14 Bloom Reveal: compact opens NOT by human hand but by its own mechanical unfolding — halves separating, rotating 120 degrees outward like a brass flower opening, revealing the golden powder inside as the "bloom."

Fill: White wall bounce at -1.5 stops (gallery walls as giant reflectors), ambient and clean. Rim: None needed (clean white environment provides separation). Product at 2+ stops brighter than Aira (receiving direct overhead beam). Light separation: Product in spotlight, Aira in ambient.

### Frame 4 — Application on Cheekbone (Poetry Fragment)

ASPECT RATIO: 9:16 vertical. SUBJECT: AIRA — Adult woman late 20s-early 30s, South Asian (Indian), warm honey-to-caramel skin tone with golden undertone, 5'6"-5'8", soft-strong hourglass-athletic silhouette, fuller sculpted legs with toned thigh definition, fuller shapely thighs, fuller feminine arms with subtle muscle tone, fuller defined chest in proportion, flat toned midsection, defined waist clear waist-to-hip ratio, curvy hip line with natural feminine flare, heart-shaped to oval face, defined cheekbones, full defined lips with natural cupid's bow, almond-shaped expressive eyes dark brown iris with subtle amber flecks, strong but feminine groomed naturally arched brow, natural sun-kissed glow, long dark brown to near-black hair with subtle warm highlights naturally textured soft waves with body and movement, elegant well-groomed hands. The chrome-and-gold combination emerging.

LEFT cheekbone still matte (showing the before/after contrast). Breath — exhale with the whispered word.

KINETIC STILLNESS: 1. Ring-finger mid-press on cheekbone (product transferring, shimmer depositing, visible point-of-contact) 2. Silver dress catching light as before, hair bun geometric and controlled 3. Golden shimmer particles on cheekbone creating own micro-atmosphere of light around application point 4. Finger pressing into cheekbone creating skin-flex and product-deposit simultaneously 5. Gallery space unchanged, overhead light constant 6. ### Frame 6 — Final (Gallery Exit)

ASPECT RATIO: 9:16 vertical. SUBJECT: AIRA — Adult woman late 20s-early 30s, South Asian (Indian), warm honey-to-caramel skin tone with golden undertone, 5'6"-5'8", soft-strong hourglass-athletic silhouette, fuller sculpted legs with toned thigh definition, fuller shapely thighs, fuller feminine arms with subtle muscle tone, fuller defined chest in proportion, flat toned midsection, defined waist clear waist-to-hip ratio, curvy hip line with natural feminine flare, heart-shaped to oval face, defined cheekbones, full defined lips with natural cupid's bow, almond-shaped expressive eyes dark brown iris with subtle amber flecks, strong but feminine groomed naturally arched brow, natural sun-kissed glow, long dark brown to near-black hair with subtle warm highlights naturally textured soft waves with body and movement, elegant well-groomed hands. WARDROBE/HAIR/MAKEUP: Complete. Full editorial beauty look.

PRODUCT STATE: Left on pedestal (returned to art-object state, closed, sculptural). Aira walking AWAY from it — the product has done its work, now she carries it on her face as she exits.

HAND POSITIONS: Both at sides in stride, fingers slightly spread with architectural grace, arms with natural walking motion.

FACIAL MICRO-DYNAMICS: Eyes — looking forward (into gallery exit/distance), not at camera, the profile revealing cheekbone highlight catching light as she moves through the space, chrome lid visible at angle. The face as lit-from-within editorial final.

BODY POSTURE: MID-STRIDE walking away from pedestal toward gallery exit/archway. Weight on right, left leg mid-step forward. Silver dress in motion catching overhead skylights along geometric folds. The editorial walking-shot departure.

KINETIC STILLNESS — Six Layers:
1. Subject mid-stride away from pedestal (left leg forward, heel about to land, right pushing off), the departure captured in motion
2. Silver dress catching and releasing overhead light with each stride-motion, fabric in angular movement, bun absolutely still contrasting with body-motion
3. Gallery air particles catching light in her wake (suggestion of movement through space)
4. Left heel approaching floor (about to make contact), right ball-of-foot pushing with visible calf-engagement, silver heels on pale wood
5. Product on pedestal behind her (RETURNED, art-object again, static while she moves), creating narrative bookend
6. Overhead skylights creating moving shadow below her as she passes through multiple light-pools in gallery space

SPATIAL LOGIC: FG: Gallery floor and architectural element (archway edge) slightly soft. MG: Aira mid-stride in profile, sharp, highlighted face catching light. BG: Product on pedestal in the space she's leaving (visible but smaller with distance), white gallery walls, overhead light beams.

LIGHTING: MULTIPLE overhead skylights in gallery — Aira walking through them creates shifting light quality on face and dress. Each skylight a new pool of light. Highlights on face catching at different angles with each stride. The product performing as she moves through various lighting conditions.

FRAMING: Full Shot — head to heels with gallery architecture. Subject 45%. Gallery scale visible. The wide editorial departure with product visible behind in context.

LENS: 35mm. f/2.8. Full gallery depth sharp.

COMPOSITION: Leading line of gallery archway drawing eye to exit, Kubrick one-point perspective with receding gallery, product left behind as punctuation in the departing narrative.

ATMOSPHERE: Gallery editorial departure, the conclusion of the beauty-film, the product's work complete and carried on her face as she re-enters the world, clean and architectural and final. Maximum restraint and control.

COLOR GRADE: High-key whites, silver dress catching pools of overhead light, golden-champagne highlights reading as only warm accent in otherwise cool-silver world, controlled and editorial to the last frame. Chrome-accented precision.

NEGATIVE: mirrored, flipped, inverted, extra limbs, fused fingers, melted features, asymmetric eyes (unintentional), garbled text, floating shadows, duplicated subjects, low-res patches, plastic skin, oversharpened, AI-generated artifacts, watermarks, signature, deformed hands, malformed teeth, joint cuts at ankle/knee/wrist/elbow/neck, amputated fingertips, cross-eyed, lazy eye, off-axis pupils, melted clothing, shoes-not-touching-ground, mismatched footwear pair, mannequin-stiff posture, dead eyes, statue-frozen energy.

## VIDEO PROMPTS

### Frame 1 — Video (Gallery Establishing)

SHOT TYPE: Full Shot. CAMERA MOVEMENT: Slow orbit CW (quarter-turn over 5s, establishing the gallery space and Aira beside product-on-pedestal). LENS: 35mm. SUBJECT ACTION: Aira standing beside pedestal with closed compact, gallery stillness. Minimal movement — just the contemplative presence. Slight weight-shift at 3.0s. LIGHTING: Overhead skylight beam on product, gallery whites. ENVIRONMENT: Minimalist gallery — white walls, single skylight, pale floor, pedestal, negative space. AUDIO: Pure ambient — gallery silence (the most quiet sound design), subtle HVAC hum, footstep-settling at 3.0s, skylight-beam has almost-audible warmth. NO MUSIC. Duration: ~5s. Frame rate: 24fps. Motion blur: 180-degree shutter (cinematic standard). Orbit smooth and reverent. Lip-sync: N/A (no speech).

NEGATIVE: morphing, warping, identity drift, limb teleport, object pop-in, frame skip, mirrored composition, text overlay, watermark, AI artifact, ghosting, double exposure unless intended, lip-sync drift, audio desync, wardrobe drift between shots, unmotivated camera shake, physics violation (water/fire/hair/fabric), mannequin posture, frozen background, identity flicker.

### Frame 2 — Video (Bloom Reveal)

SHOT TYPE: Product CU. CAMERA MOVEMENT: Vertical tilt up (starting at product-level on pedestal, product-centered, capturing the bloom-reveal happening over 5s). LENS: 50mm. SUBJECT ACTION: Compact on pedestal — at 1.0s begins P-14 Bloom Reveal (magnetic closure releases, halves begin separating and rotating outward). Over 2.5s the full bloom unfolds (0 to 120 degrees). Formula revealed, catching skylight, golden shimmer visible. At 4.0s camera begins tilt up toward Aira's reaction face. LIGHTING: Overhead beam catching the revealing formula, golden light projecting upward from newly-exposed shimmer surface. ENVIRONMENT: Gallery, pedestal, revealing product. AUDIO: Gallery ambient + mechanical bloom sounds (satisfying magnetic release click at 1.0s, subtle brass-hinge whisper as halves rotate, shimmer-catch — almost crystalline subtle ring as formula catches light). Duration: ~5s. Frame rate: 24fps. Motion blur: 180-degree shutter (cinematic standard). Lip-sync: N/A (no speech).

NEGATIVE: morphing, warping, identity drift, limb teleport, object pop-in, frame skip, mirrored composition, text overlay, watermark, AI artifact, ghosting, double exposure unless intended, lip-sync drift, audio desync, wardrobe drift between shots, unmotivated camera shake, physics violation (water/fire/hair/fabric), mannequin posture, frozen background, identity flicker.
